// --- Sub-Component: AddLocationModal ---
const AddLocationModal = ({ isOpen, onClose }) => {
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({ code: "", name: "" });
  const [isRoleModalOpen, setIsRoleModalOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isSigModalOpen, setIsSigModalOpen] = useState(false);

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  const handleSave = async () => {
    try {
      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/add-location', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(formData)
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      if (data.success) {
        alert("Location saved successfully!");
        onClose();
      }
    } catch (err) {
      alert("Error connecting to server");
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="modal-overlay">
      <div className="location-modal">
        <div className="modal-header">
          <span>Add New Location</span>
          <button onClick={onClose} className="close-x">&times;</button>
        </div>
        <div className="modal-body">
          <input 
            type="text" 
            placeholder="Code (e.g. MYL001)" 
            onChange={(e) => setFormData({...formData, code: e.target.value})} 
          />
          <input 
            type="text" 
            placeholder="Location Name" 
            onChange={(e) => setFormData({...formData, name: e.target.value})} 
          />
          <button className="submit-modal-btn" onClick={handleSave}>Save Location</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// --- Main Component ---
function Home() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [selectedRole, setSelectedRole] = useState("");
  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false); 
  const [isAddModalOpen, setIsAddModalOpen] = useState(false); 

  // ADD THESE TWO LINES HERE:
  const [isRoleModalOpen, setIsRoleModalOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isSigModalOpen, setIsSigModalOpen] = useState(false);

  // ADD THIS FUNCTION BACK:
  const handleLogout = () => {
    localStorage.removeItem("userRole");
    localStorage.removeItem("userToken");
    navigate('/');
  };

  const handleActionClick = (itemName) => {
    if (itemName === "FrontDesk") {
      navigate('/frontdesk');
    } else if (itemName === "Sample Collect") {
      setIsModalOpen(true);
    } else if (itemName === "Customer Care") { 
      navigate('/customer-care'); // Correct place for Customer Care
    } else if (itemName === "PatientDetails") {
      navigate('/add-patient');
    } 
    else {
      console.log(`${itemName} clicked`);
    }
  };

  const handleTableOpClick = (desc) => {
    if (desc === "Add Location") {
      setIsAddModalOpen(true);
    } 
    else if (desc === "Add Role") {
      setIsRoleModalOpen(true);
    } 
    else if (desc === "Upload Signature") {
      setIsSigModalOpen(true);
    } 
    else if (desc === "Add Out Of Hospital") { 
      navigate('/add-out-of-hospital');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Group") {
      navigate('/add-group'); 
    }
    else if (desc === "View Location") {
      navigate('/view-location');
    } 
    else if (desc === "Create User") {
      navigate('/create-user');
    } 
    else if (desc === "Add Title") {
      navigate('/titles');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add CollectedAt") {
      navigate('/collected-at');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Insurance") {
      navigate('/add-insurance');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Doctors Details") {
      navigate('/add-doctor');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add PatientDetails") {
      navigate('/add-patient');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Client Code") {
      navigate('/add-client-code');
    }
    else if (desc === "Display Codes") {
      navigate('/display-codes'); 
    }
    else {
      alert(`${desc} module is coming soon!`);
    }
  };

  const handleModalSubmit = (code) => {
    setIsModalOpen(false);
    navigate('/sample-collect', { state: { locationCode: code } });
  };

  return (
    <div className="home-wrapper">
      <header className="brand-nav" style={{ 
    backgroundColor: '#4a148c', 
    display: 'flex', 
    alignItems: 'center', 
    padding: '10px 20px',
    color: 'white',
    position: 'relative' // Useful for absolute centering
}}>
  {/* 1. Left Spacer (matches the width of the right section to keep title dead-center) */}
  <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
     {/* You can put a logo or home icon here if needed later */}
  </div>

  {/* 2. Center Title */}
  <h3 className="nav-title" style={{ 
      margin: 0, 
      textAlign: 'center', 
      flex: 2, 
      whiteSpace: 'nowrap' 
  }}>
      Patho Consult Portal
  </h3>
  
  {/* 3. Right Section */}
  <div className="nav-right-section" style={{ flex: 1, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
    <button 
      className="logout-btn-box" 
      onClick={handleLogout}
      style={{
          backgroundColor: '#ffffff', 
          color: '#4a148c',          
          border: 'none',
          padding: '6px 18px',
          borderRadius: '4px',
          cursor: 'pointer',
          fontWeight: 'bold',
          fontSize: '14px',
          transition: '0.3s'
      }}
      onMouseOver={(e) => e.target.style.backgroundColor = '#f3e5f5'}
      onMouseOut={(e) => e.target.style.backgroundColor = '#ffffff'}
    >
      Logout
    </button>
  </div>
</header>
      <main className="dashboard-content">
        <h2 className="welcome-banner">Welcome To Patho Clinic</h2>
        
        <section className="admin-panel">
          <div className="panel-row">
            <label>Select Admin Operation</label>
            <select 
              className="purple-select" 
              value={selectedRole} 
              onChange={(e) => setSelectedRole(e.target.value)}
            >
              <option value="">-- Select User Role --</option>
              <option value="Admin">Admin</option>
              <option value="Registration">Registration</option>
              <option value="Lab">Lab</option>
              <option value="Invoice">Invoice</option>
            </select>
          </div>

          {selectedRole && (
            <div className="operation-table-container">
              <table className="operation-table">
                <thead>
                  <tr>
                    <th>S.No</th>
                    <th>Description</th>
                    <th>Action</th>
                  </tr>
                </thead>
<tbody key={selectedRole}>
  {roleOperations[selectedRole].map((op) => (
    <tr key={op.sNo}>
      <td>{op.sNo}</td>
      <td>{op.desc}</td>
      <td>
        <button 
          className="view-page-btn"
          onClick={() => handleTableOpClick(op.desc)}
        >
          {op.page}
        </button>
      </td>
    </tr>
  ))}
</tbody>
              </table>
              <button className="innovative-btn">Trigger Cron</button>
            </div>
          )}
        </section>

        <div className="action-list">
          {menuItems.map((item) => (
            <div 
              key={item.name} 
              className="action-row" 
              onClick={() => handleActionClick(item.name)}
            >
              <span className="action-text">
                {item.name} 
                {item.badge && <span className="purple-badge">{item.badge}</span>}
              </span>
              <span className="action-chevron">›</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </main>

      {/* --- MODALS SECTION --- */}
      {/* 1. Find Location */}
      <LocationModal 
        isOpen={isModalOpen} 
        onClose={() => setIsModalOpen(false)} 
        onConfirm={handleModalSubmit}
      />

      {/* 2. Add Location */}
      <AddLocationModal 
        isOpen={isAddModalOpen} 
        onClose={() => setIsAddModalOpen(false)} 
      />

      {/* 3. Add Role */}
      <AddRoleModal 
        isOpen={isRoleModalOpen} 
        onClose={() => setIsRoleModalOpen(false)} 
      />

      {/* 4. Upload Signature */}
      <UploadSignatureModal 
        isOpen={isSigModalOpen} 
        onClose={() => setIsSigModalOpen(false)} 
      />
      
      <footer className="footer-bar">
        System Status: Secure | Connected to Diagnostics Cloud
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

    e.preventDefault();
    
    // Log for debugging

        const response = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/add-test', {
            method: 'POST',

        });

        const result = await response.json();

        if (result.success) {

        } else {
            alert("Error: " + result.error);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Connection error:", error);
        alert("Server is not responding. Check if your Node.js backend is running on port 5000.");
    }
};

        setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, selectedProfile: profile }));

                <div style={{ backgroundColor: '#f8f9fa', padding: '12px 20px', borderBottom: '1px solid #3e4d5c' }}>

                    <div style={{ backgroundColor: 'white', padding: '25px', borderRadius: '8px', width: '350px', boxShadow: '0 10px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)' }}>
                        <h4 style={{ marginTop: 0, color: '#005f6b', borderBottom: '2px solid #005f6b', paddingBottom: '10px' }}>Select Master Profile</h4>
                        <div style={{ maxHeight: '250px', overflowY: 'auto', margin: '15px 0' }}>
                            {dropdownData.profiles.map((p) => (
                                <div 
                                    key={p} 
                                    onClick={() => handleProfileSelect(p)}
                                    style={{ padding: '10px', cursor: 'pointer', borderBottom: '1px solid #f0f0f0', transition: '0.2s' }}
                                    onMouseOver={(e) => e.target.style.backgroundColor = '#eefaff'}
                                    onMouseOut={(e) => e.target.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent'}
                                >
                                    📁 {p}
                                </div>
                            ))}
                        </div>
                        <button onClick={() => setShowProfileModal(false)} style={{ width: '100%', padding: '10px', backgroundColor: '#666', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '4px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>Cancel</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            )}

            <footer style={{ position: 'fixed', bottom: 0, width: '100%', backgroundColor: '#005f6b', color: 'white', fontSize: '10px', textAlign: 'center', padding: '8px 0' }}>
                63, Appu street, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004. Phone:044-24934435 | pathoconsult@gmail.com
            </footer>
        </div>
    );
};

const InputGroup = ({ label, name, required, onChange, list, options, showPlus }) => (
    <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}>
        <label style={{ fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>
            {label} {required && <span style={{ color: 'red' }}>*</span>}
        </label>
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '5px', marginTop: '4px' }}>
            <input name={name} list={list} onChange={onChange} autoComplete="off" style={{ flex: 1, padding: '5px', border: '1px solid #ccc', borderRadius: '3px' }} required={required} />
            {options && <datalist id={list}>{options.map((opt, i) => <option key={i} value={opt} />)}</datalist>}
            {showPlus && <button type="button" style={{ backgroundColor: '#4caf50', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '50%', width: '25px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>+</button>}
        </div>
    </div>
);

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import "../styles/home.css";


import { Box } from '@mui/material'; 
import { DataGrid, GridToolbar } from '@mui/x-data-grid';

function CustomerCare() {
    const navigate = useNavigate();
    const [dates, setDates] = useState({ from: '', to: '' });
    const [data, setData] = useState([]);
    // State to handle the Preview Screen
    const [selectedPatient, setSelectedPatient] = useState(null);
    const [showEmailModal, setShowEmailModal] = useState(false);

    const handleSearch = async () => {
        if (!dates.from || !dates.to) {
            alert("Please select both From and To dates.");
            return;
        }

        try {
            const response = await fetch(
                `http://localhost:5000/api/customer-view-full?fromDate=${dates.from}&toDate=${dates.to}`
            );
            const result = await response.json();
            
            if (result.success) {
    // Adds a unique id to each row for the DataGrid
    const rowsWithId = result.data.map((row, index) => ({
        ...row,
        id: row.sample_id || index 
    }));
    setData(rowsWithId);
} else {
                alert("Error fetching data: " + result.message);
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error("Fetch error:", error);
            alert("Connection failed. Ensure the backend server is running on port 5000.");
        }
    };
    const handleSendMail = async () => {
    try {
        const response = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/send-report-mail', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                email: selectedPatient.email || 'recipient@example.com', // Replace with actual email field
                sampleId: selectedPatient.sample_id,
                patientName: selectedPatient.patient_name,
                // Pass the data needed for the PDF generation
                reportData: selectedPatient 
            })
        });

        const result = await response.json();
        if (result.success) {
            alert("✅ Mail sent successfully with the report attachment!");
            setShowEmailModal(false);
            setSelectedPatient(null);
        } else {
            alert("❌ Failed to send mail: " + result.error);
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Mail error:", error);
        alert("Connection error while sending mail.");
    }
};

    const actionBtnStyle = {
        border: '1px solid #ccc',
        background: '#fff',
        cursor: 'pointer',
        padding: '2px 6px',
        borderRadius: '4px',
        fontSize: '14px'
    };

    return (
        <div className="home-wrapper" style={{ backgroundColor: '#4a148c', minHeight: '100vh', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}>
            <header className="brand-nav" style={{ backgroundColor: '#4a148c', color: 'white', padding: '10px' }}>
                <h3 style={{ margin: 0, textAlign: 'center', width: '100%' }}>Patho Consult</h3>
                <span style={{ float: 'right', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '20px' }} onClick={() => navigate('/home')}>🏠</span>
            </header>

            <main style={{ padding: '20px', flex: 1 }}>
                {/* Search Panel */}
                <div className="admin-panel" style={{ maxWidth: '600px', margin: '0 auto', borderRadius: '15px', overflow: 'hidden', boxShadow: '0 4px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2)' }}>
                    <div style={{ backgroundColor: '#eee', padding: '10px', textAlign: 'center', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Search by Date</div>
                    <div style={{ padding: '15px', backgroundColor: 'white' }}>
                        <label>From Date</label>
                        <input type="date" className="purple-select" style={{ width: '100%', marginBottom: '10px' }} 
                               onChange={e => setDates({...dates, from: e.target.value})} />
                        
                        <label>To Date</label>
                        <input type="date" className="purple-select" style={{ width: '100%', marginBottom: '15px' }} 
                               onChange={e => setDates({...dates, to: e.target.value})} />
                        
                        <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>
                            <button style={{ backgroundColor: '#8e44ad', color: 'white', border: 'none', padding: '10px 25px', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer' }} onClick={handleSearch}>Search</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                {/* --- NEW DATA GRID --- */}
<Box sx={{ 
    height: 600, 
    width: '100%', 
    mt: 4, 
    backgroundColor: 'white', 
    borderRadius: '8px',
    p: 1,
    boxShadow: '0 4px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)'
}}>
    <DataGrid
        rows={data}
        columns={[
            { field: 'patient_name', headerName: 'Patient Name', width: 180, renderCell: (params) => <b style={{color: '#27ae60'}}>{params.value}</b> },
            { field: 'lab_status', headerName: 'Lab Status', width: 120 },
            { field: 'status', headerName: 'Status', width: 120 },
            { field: 'PatientID', headerName: 'Patient ID', width: 120 },
            { field: 'sample_id', headerName: 'Sample ID', width: 130 },
            { field: 'referred_by', headerName: 'Referred By', width: 150 },
            { field: 'collected_at', headerName: 'Collected At', width: 180 },
            { field: 'test_completed', headerName: 'Completed', width: 130 },
            { 
                field: 'actions', 
                headerName: 'Action', 
                width: 220,

                        <button title="Final" style={{ ...actionBtnStyle, color: 'green' }} onClick={() => setSelectedPatient({ ...params.row, mode: 'final' })}>✅</button>
                        <button title="Send Mail" style={{ ...actionBtnStyle, color: 'blue' }} onClick={() => { setSelectedPatient(params.row); setShowEmailModal(true); }}>✉️</button>
                    </div>
                ) 
            }
        ]}
        slots={{ toolbar: GridToolbar }}
        pageSizeOptions={[10, 25, 50]}
        initialState={{ pagination: { paginationModel: { pageSize: 10 } } }}
        disableRowSelectionOnClick
    />
</Box>

                {/* --- REPORT PREVIEW MODAL --- */}
{selectedPatient && !showEmailModal && (

            <div style={{ backgroundColor: 'white', margin: '0 20px 15px 20px', padding: '25px', borderRadius: '8px' }}>

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { Box, Typography, TextField, Button, Paper } from '@mui/material';
import { DataGrid, GridToolbar } from '@mui/x-data-grid';

function LabView() {
    const navigate = useNavigate();
    const [dates, setDates] = useState({ 
        from: '2024-01-01', 
        to: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] 
    });
    const [rows, setRows] = useState([]);
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

    const fetchLabData = async (fromDate, toDate) => {
        setLoading(true);
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`http://localhost:5000/api/lab-view-data?fromDate=${fromDate}&toDate=${toDate}`);
            const result = await response.json();
            if (result.success) {
                const rowsWithId = result.data.map((row, index) => ({
                    ...row,
                    id: row.sample_id || `temp-${index}` 
                }));
                setRows(rowsWithId);
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error("Fetch error:", error);
        } finally {
            setLoading(false);
        }
    };

    useEffect(() => {
        fetchLabData(dates.from, dates.to);
    }, []);

    const handleSearch = () => {
        if (!dates.from || !dates.to) return alert("Please select dates.");
        fetchLabData(dates.from, dates.to);
    };

    const columns = [
        { 
            field: 'patient_name', 
            headerName: 'Patient Name', 
            minWidth: 180, 
            flex: 1.5, // Flex makes the column expand to fill space
            renderCell: (params) => (
                <span style={{ color: '#4a148c', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>{params.value}</span>
            )
        },
        { field: 'patient_id', headerName: 'Patient ID', width: 120 },
        { field: 'external_id', headerName: 'External ID', width: 120 },
        { field: 'collected_at', headerName: 'Collected At', width: 180 },
        { field: 'client_code', headerName: 'Client Code', width: 130 },
        { field: 'lab_status', headerName: 'Lab Status', width: 130 },
        { field: 'status', headerName: 'Status', width: 120 },
        { field: 'test_billed', headerName: 'Billed', type: 'number', width: 100 },
        { field: 'confirmed_test', headerName: 'Confirmed', type: 'number', width: 110 },
        { field: 'approved_test', headerName: 'Approved', type: 'number', width: 110 },
        { field: 'sample_id', headerName: 'Sample ID', width: 150 },
    ];

    return (
        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', minHeight: '100vh', width: '100%', bgcolor: '#f0cdf5' }}>
            {/* Header */}
            <Box sx={{ p: 2, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', color: 'white', bgcolor: '#4a148c', position: 'relative' }}>
                <Typography variant="h5" fontWeight="bold">Patho Consult - Lab View</Typography>
                <Button onClick={() => navigate('/home')} sx={{ position: 'absolute', right: 20, color: 'white', fontSize: '24px' }}>🏠</Button>
            </Box>

            {/* Content Area */}
            <Box sx={{ p: 1, flex: 1, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}>
                {/* Search Bar - Slimmer to give table more room */}
                <Paper sx={{ p: 1.5, mb: 1, display: 'flex', gap: 2, justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', borderRadius: '4px' }}>
                    <TextField label="From" type="date" size="small" value={dates.from} InputLabelProps={{ shrink: true }} onChange={(e) => setDates({...dates, from: e.target.value})} />
                    <TextField label="To" type="date" size="small" value={dates.to} InputLabelProps={{ shrink: true }} onChange={(e) => setDates({...dates, to: e.target.value})} />
                    <Button variant="contained" onClick={handleSearch} sx={{ bgcolor: '#4a148c', '&:hover': { bgcolor: '#6a1b9a' } }}>Search Data</Button>
                </Paper>

                {/* The Broad Table Container */}
                <Box sx={{ 
                    flex: 1, 
                    width: '100%',
                    height: 'calc(100vh - 200px)', // Auto-adjust height based on header/footer
                    bgcolor: 'white', 
                    boxShadow: 3,
                    '& .MuiDataGrid-root': { 
                        border: '1px solid #ccc',
                        borderRadius: '0px' // Sharp edges for a professional broader look
                    },
                    '& .MuiDataGrid-columnHeaders': { 
                        bgcolor: '#f3e5f5', 
                        color: '#4a148c',
                        borderBottom: '2px solid #4a148c', // Stronger border for header
                        fontSize: '14px'
                    },
                    '& .MuiDataGrid-cell': { 
                        borderBottom: '1px solid #e0e0e0',
                        borderRight: '1px solid #f0f0f0', // Column separators
                        fontSize: '13px'
                    },
                    '& .MuiDataGrid-columnHeader': {
                        borderRight: '1px solid #ccc' // Header separators
                    },
                    '& .MuiDataGrid-row:hover': { 
                        bgcolor: '#f7dffa !important' 
                    },
                    // Header Filter customization
                    '& .MuiDataGrid-headerFilterRow': {
                        bgcolor: '#fafafa',
                    }
                }}>
                    <DataGrid
                        rows={rows}
                        columns={columns}
                        loading={loading}
                        unstable_headerFilters={true} 
                        slots={{ toolbar: GridToolbar }}
                        slotProps={{
                            toolbar: { 
                                showQuickFilter: true,
                                sx: { p: 1, bgcolor: '#fdfdfd', borderBottom: '1px solid #ccc' } 
                            }
                        }}
                        density="compact"
                        disableRowSelectionOnClick
                    />
                </Box>
            </Box>
            
            {/* Footer */}
            <Box sx={{ p: 1, color: 'white', textAlign: 'center', bgcolor: '#4a148c', fontSize: '12px' }}>
                63, Appu street, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004. | Phone: 044-24934435
            </Box>
        </Box>
    );
}

export default LabView;




import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { 
  FaUserMd, FaGraduationCap, FaFileSignature, 
  FaCalendarAlt, FaUniversity, FaUserTag 
} from 'react-icons/fa'; // Install react-icons
import "../styles/home.css"; 

const UploadSignatureModal = ({ isOpen, onClose }) => {
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    userName: "", firstName: "", lastName: "", gender: "",
    dob: "", age: "", undergraduateDegree: "", ugUniversity: "",
    postgraduateDegree: "", pgUniversity: "", college: "",
    otherDegree: "", registrationNumber: "", designation: "",
    designationCategory: "", designationForReport: ""
  });
  const [file, setFile] = useState(null);
  const [preview, setPreview] = useState(null);

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  const handleInputChange = (e) => {
    const { name, value } = e.target;
    setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [name]: value }));
  };

  const handleFileChange = (e) => {
    const selectedFile = e.target.files[0];
    setFile(selectedFile);
    if (selectedFile) {
      setPreview(URL.createObjectURL(selectedFile));
    }
  };

  const handleSubmit = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const data = new FormData();
    Object.keys(formData).forEach(key => data.append(key, formData[key]));
    if (file) data.append('signature', file);

    try {
      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/register-pathologist', {
        method: 'POST',
        body: data,
      });
      const result = await response.json();
      if (result.success) {
        alert("Pathologist Profile Created Successfully!");
        onClose();
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Submission error:", error);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="modal-overlay" style={{ background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.7)', backdropFilter: 'blur(4px)' }}>
      <div className="signature-modal-container" style={{ 
        width: '85%', maxWidth: '1100px', borderRadius: '15px', border: 'none', boxShadow: '0 20px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.3)' 
      }}>
        
        {/* Modern Header */}
        <div className="modal-header-teal" style={{ 
          background: '#1a5f5f', padding: '20px 30px', borderTopLeftRadius: '15px', borderTopRightRadius: '15px',
          display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center'
        }}>
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px', color: 'white' }}>
            <FaUserMd size={24} />
            <h2 style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: '1.2rem', fontWeight: 600 }}>Pathologist Registration</h2>
          </div>
          <button onClick={onClose} style={{ background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)', border: 'none', color: 'white', fontSize: '20px', cursor: 'pointer', borderRadius: '50%', width: '35px', height: '35px' }}>&times;</button>
        </div>

        <div className="modal-scroll-body" style={{ padding: '30px', backgroundColor: '#fdfdfd' }}>
          
          <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
            {/* Section 1: Personal Details */}
            <div style={{ marginBottom: '25px' }}>
              <h4 style={{ color: '#1a5f5f', borderBottom: '2px solid #eee', paddingBottom: '8px', marginBottom: '20px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '8px' }}>
                <FaUserTag /> Personal Information
              </h4>
              <div className="signature-grid" style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(3, 1fr)', gap: '20px' }}>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>User Name</label>
                  <input type="text" name="userName" onChange={handleInputChange} placeholder="Unique ID" />
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>First Name <span style={{color: 'red'}}>*</span></label>
                  <input type="text" name="firstName" required onChange={handleInputChange} />
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>Last Name</label>
                  <input type="text" name="lastName" onChange={handleInputChange} />
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>Date of Birth</label>
                  <input type="date" name="dob" onChange={handleInputChange} />
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>Gender</label>
                  <select name="gender" onChange={handleInputChange}>
                    <option value="">Select</option>
                    <option value="Male">Male</option>
                    <option value="Female">Female</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>Age</label>
                  <input type="number" name="age" onChange={handleInputChange} />
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Section 2: Academic & Professional */}
            <div style={{ marginBottom: '25px' }}>
              <h4 style={{ color: '#1a5f5f', borderBottom: '2px solid #eee', paddingBottom: '8px', marginBottom: '20px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '8px' }}>
                <FaGraduationCap /> Academic & Registration
              </h4>
              <div className="signature-grid" style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(3, 1fr)', gap: '20px' }}>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>Undergraduate Degree</label>
                  <input type="text" name="undergraduateDegree" placeholder="e.g. MBBS" onChange={handleInputChange} />
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label><FaUniversity style={{fontSize: '10px'}}/> UG University</label>
                  <input type="text" name="ugUniversity" onChange={handleInputChange} />
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>Registration No.</label>
                  <input type="text" name="registrationNumber" onChange={handleInputChange} />
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>Postgraduate Degree</label>
                  <input type="text" name="postgraduateDegree" onChange={handleInputChange} />
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>PG University</label>
                  <input type="text" name="pgUniversity" onChange={handleInputChange} />
                </div>
                <div className="form-group-modern">
                  <label>Designation Category</label>
                  <select name="designationCategory" onChange={handleInputChange}>
                    <option value="">-- Select --</option>
                    <option value="Pathologist">Pathologist</option>
                    <option value="Micro Biologist">Micro Biologist</option>
                  </select>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Section 3: Signature & Reports */}
            <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1.5fr 1fr', gap: '30px', marginTop: '30px' }}>
              <div style={{ padding: '20px', background: '#f8fbfb', borderRadius: '10px', border: '1px dashed #1a5f5f' }}>
                <h4 style={{ margin: '0 0 15px 0', color: '#1a5f5f' }}><FaFileSignature /> Digital Signature</h4>
                <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '20px', alignItems: 'center' }}>
                  <div className="custom-file-upload">
                    <input type="file" onChange={handleFileChange} id="sig-upload" hidden />
                    <label htmlFor="sig-upload" style={{ 
                      backgroundColor: '#1a5f5f', color: 'white', padding: '10px 20px', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer' 
                    }}>Choose File</label>
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: '#666' }}>
                    Max 30kB | 397 x 381 px
                  </div>
                </div>
                {preview && <img src={preview} alt="Preview" style={{ marginTop: '15px', height: '80px', border: '1px solid #ddd' }} />}
              </div>

              <div className="form-group-modern">
                <label style={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Designation for Report <span style={{color: 'red'}}>*</span></label>
                <textarea 
                  name="designationForReport" 
                  rows="4" 
                  style={{ width: '100%', borderRadius: '8px', border: '1px solid #ddd', padding: '10px' }}
                  placeholder="How should your name and degree appear on the final report?"
                  onChange={handleInputChange}
                ></textarea>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="modal-footer-btns" style={{ marginTop: '40px', textAlign: 'right', borderTop: '1px solid #eee', paddingTop: '20px' }}>
              <button type="button" onClick={onClose} style={{ marginRight: '15px', background: '#eee', border: 'none', padding: '12px 25px', borderRadius: '8px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>Cancel</button>
              <button type="submit" className="submit-btn-blue" style={{ background: '#1a5f5f', color: 'white', border: 'none', padding: '12px 40px', borderRadius: '8px', fontWeight: 'bold', cursor: 'pointer', boxShadow: '0 4px 10px rgba(26,95,95,0.3)' }}>
                Register Pathologist
              </button>
            </div>
          </form>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const pdf = require('html-pdf');

app.get('/api/generate-report/:sampleId', (req, res) => {
    const { sampleId } = req.params;

    // We use LEFT JOIN so if doctor/location is missing, the patient is still found
    const sql = `
        SELECT p.*, 
               IFNULL(d.doctor_name, 'Self') AS doctor_name, 
               IFNULL(ca.name, 'Main Center') AS collection_center
        FROM patients p
        LEFT JOIN doctor_details d ON p.doctor_id = d.id
        LEFT JOIN collected_at ca ON p.PatientID = ca.id 
        WHERE p.sample_id = ?
    `;

    db.query(sql, [sampleId], (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Database Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).send("Database Error");
        }
        
        // This is where your previous error was triggered
        if (results.length === 0) {
            return res.status(404).send(`Error: No patient found with Sample ID: ${sampleId}`);
        }
        
        const data = results[0];

        // HTML Template for the PDF
        const htmlTemplate = `
        <html>
            <body style="font-family: sans-serif; padding: 30px;">
                <div style="border-bottom: 2px solid purple; margin-bottom: 20px;">
                    <h1 style="color: purple; margin: 0;">Patho Consult</h1>
                    <p>Mylapore, Chennai | Phone: 044-24934435</p>
                </div>
                <table style="width: 100%; margin-bottom: 30px; font-size: 14px;">
                    <tr>
                        <td><strong>Name:</strong> ${data.patient_name}</td>
                        <td><strong>Age/Sex:</strong> ${data.age} / ${data.gender}</td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                        <td><strong>Patient ID:</strong> ${data.PatientID}</td>
                        <td><strong>Sample ID:</strong> ${data.sample_id}</td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                        <td><strong>Referred By:</strong> ${data.doctor_name}</td>
                        <td><strong>Date:</strong> ${data.RegDate}</td>
                    </tr>
                </table>
                <div style="margin-top: 40px;">
                    <h3>Test: Culture and Sensitivity</h3>
                    <p><strong>Specimen:</strong> Pus</p>
                    <p><strong>Result:</strong> No significant pathogen grown in culture.</p>
                </div>
                <div style="margin-top: 100px;">
                    <p><strong>${data.doctor_name}</strong><br>MD, PhD.</p>
                </div>
            </body>
        </html>`;

        const options = { format: 'A4' };

        pdf.create(htmlTemplate, options).toStream((err, stream) => {
            if (err) return res.status(500).send(err);
            res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/pdf');
            res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', `inline; filename=${sampleId}.pdf`);
            stream.pipe(res);
        });
    });
});

// 3. AUTHENTICATION ROUTE
app.post('/api/authenticate', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password, pin } = req.body;
  const sql = "SELECT * FROM login WHERE Username = ?";
  
  db.execute(sql, [username], async (err, results) => {
    if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error" });
    if (results.length === 0) return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: "User not found" });

    const user = results[0];
    const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.Password);
    
    if (!passwordMatch) {
      return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: "Invalid password" });
    }

    if (user.Username.toLowerCase() === 'admin') {
      const pinMatch = await bcrypt.compare(String(pin), user.Pin);
      if (!pinMatch) return res.status(403).json({ success: false, message: "Invalid Admin PIN" });
    }

    res.status(200).json({ 
      success: true, 
      role: user.Role || user.Username,
      token: "session_token_" + Date.now() 
    });
  });
});

// 4. FULL REGISTRATION ROUTE (With Role & Signature)
app.post('/api/register-full', upload.single('signature'), async (req, res) => {
    const { username, password, role, isAdmin } = req.body;
    const signaturePath = req.file ? req.file.path : null;

    try {
        const hashedPw = await bcrypt.hash(password, saltRounds);
        // Defaulting empty values for phone/address/pin to satisfy existing DB constraints
        const sql = `INSERT INTO login 
            (Username, Password, Role, IsAdmin, SignaturePath, Phone, Address, Pin, ISActive) 
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, '', '', '', 1)`;
        
        db.execute(sql, [username, hashedPw, role, isAdmin, signaturePath], (err, result) => {
            if (err) {
                if (err.code === 'ER_DUP_ENTRY') return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: "Username exists." });
                return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database failure." });
            }
            res.status(200).json({ success: true });
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Encryption error." });
    }
});

        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.sqlMessage });
        
        // Log this to your Terminal to see exactly what is being sent to React
        console.log("Data sent to frontend:", results); 
        
        res.json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

app.delete('/api/delete-user/:id', (req, res) => {
    const userId = req.params.id;
    
    // Instead of DELETE, we UPDATE the active status
    const sql = "UPDATE login SET ISActive = 0 WHERE ID = ?"; 

    db.query(sql, [userId], (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Database Error:", err.sqlMessage);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.sqlMessage });
        }
        
        if (result.affectedRows === 0) {
            return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: "User not found." });
        }

        res.json({ success: true, message: "User deactivated successfully" });
    });
});

// New Pathologist Registration Route (Handling Login + User Profiles)
app.post('/api/register-pathologist', upload.single('signature'), async (req, res) => {
    const {
        userName, firstName, lastName, gender, dob, age,
        undergraduateDegree, postgraduateDegree, registrationNumber, 
        designationCategory, designationForReport
    } = req.body;

    const signaturePath = req.file ? req.file.path : null;

    // 2. Use a connection from the pool for a Transaction
    db.getConnection((err, connection) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "DB Connection Error" });

        connection.beginTransaction(async (err) => {
            try {
                // STEP A: Insert into 'login' table first
                const hashedPw = await bcrypt.hash("patho123", saltRounds); // Default password
                const loginSql = "INSERT INTO login (Username, Password, Role, ISActive) VALUES (?, ?, 'Pathologist', 1)";
                
                connection.query(loginSql, [userName, hashedPw], (err, loginResult) => {
                    if (err) {
                        return connection.rollback(() => {
                            connection.release();
                            const msg = err.code === 'ER_DUP_ENTRY' ? "Username already exists." : "Login table error.";
                            res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: msg });
                        });
                    }

                    const newUserId = loginResult.insertId; // This is the ID for user_profiles

                    // STEP B: Insert into 'user_profiles' table
                    const profileSql = `
                        INSERT INTO user_profiles 
                        (user_id, FirstName, LastName, designation, Gender, DOB, Age, 
                        UndergraduateDegree, PostgraduateDegree, RegistrationNumber, 
                        DesignationForReport, SignaturePath) 
                        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)`;

                    const profileValues = [
                        newUserId, firstName, lastName, designationCategory, gender, 
                        dob || null, age || null, undergraduateDegree, 
                        postgraduateDegree, registrationNumber, 
                        designationForReport, signaturePath
                    ];

                    connection.query(profileSql, profileValues, (err) => {
                        if (err) {
                            return connection.rollback(() => {
                                connection.release();
                                console.error("Profile Error:", err);
                                res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Error saving profile details." });
                            });
                        }

                        // STEP C: Commit both inserts
                        connection.commit((err) => {
                            if (err) return connection.rollback(() => { throw err; });
                            connection.release();
                            res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: "Pathologist registered successfully!" });
                        });
                    });
                });
            } catch (error) {
                connection.rollback(() => {
                    connection.release();
                    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Server processing error." });
                });
            }
        });
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-out-of-hospital', (req, res) => {
    // Destructure everything coming from React
    const { location, hospitalName, createDate, testProfile, amount } = req.body;

    console.log("Incoming Data:", { location, hospitalName, createDate, testProfile, amount });

    db.getConnection((err, connection) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "DB Connection Error" });

        connection.beginTransaction((err) => {
            if (err) { connection.release(); return res.status(500).json({ success: false }); }

            // STEP 1: Insert Hospital
            const sqlClient = "INSERT INTO out_of_hospital_clients (LocationCode, HospitalName, CreatedAt) VALUES (?, ?, ?)";
            connection.query(sqlClient, [location, hospitalName, createDate], (err, result) => {
                if (err) {
                    return connection.rollback(() => {
                        connection.release();
                        console.error("Client Insert Error:", err.sqlMessage);
                        res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.sqlMessage });
                    });
                }

                const clientId = result.insertId;
                
                // STEP 2: Insert Rates
                // We use || 0 to ensure the decimal column gets a number even if 'amount' is empty
                const finalAmount = amount || 0;
                const sqlRate = "INSERT INTO out_of_hospital_rates (client_id, TestProfileName, Amount) VALUES (?, ?, ?)";
                
                connection.query(sqlRate, [clientId, testProfile, finalAmount], (err) => {
                    if (err) {
                        return connection.rollback(() => {
                            connection.release();
                            console.error("Rates Insert Error:", err.sqlMessage);
                            // This will send the EXACT database error back to your browser alert
                            res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database Error: " + err.sqlMessage });
                        });
                    }

                    // STEP 3: Commit
                    connection.commit((err) => {
                        if (err) return connection.rollback(() => { throw err; });
                        connection.release();
                        res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: "Stored Successfully!" });
                    });
                });
            });
        });
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-group', (req, res) => {
    const { 
        groupName, numPersons, amount, location, 
        hospitalName, referredBy, clientCode, clientName, 
        sampleCollect, paymentMode, paidAmount, netAmount, 
        profileTest,
        // Match these to the keys you send from React handleSave
        acc_holder, acc_no, cheque_no, bank_name, trans_id, digital_mode, status 
    } = req.body;

    // Use the EXACT column names from your DESCRIBE groups; output
    const sql = `INSERT INTO groups 
        (GroupName, NumPersons, TotalAmount, ProfileTest, LocationCode, 
        HospitalName, ReferredBy, ClientCode, ClientName, SampleCollect, 
        PaymentMode, PaidAmount, NetAmount, 
        acc_holder, acc_no, cheque_no, bank_name, trans_id, digital_mode, status,
        CreatedAt) 
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NOW())`;

    const values = [
        groupName || null, 
        parseInt(numPersons) || 0, 
        parseFloat(amount) || 0, 
        profileTest || null,      // Put ProfileTest here to match SQL order
        location || null,         // LocationCode
        hospitalName || null, 
        referredBy || null, 
        clientCode || null, 
        clientName || null, 
        sampleCollect || 'No',
        paymentMode || null, 
        parseFloat(paidAmount) || 0, 
        parseFloat(netAmount) || 0,
        // Individual Columns matching the destructuring above
        acc_holder || null,
        acc_no || null,
        cheque_no || null,
        bank_name || null,
        trans_id || null,
        digital_mode || null,
        status || 'Pending'
    ];

    db.query(sql, values, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("MariaDB Error Details:", err.message); // This will tell us if columns still mismatch
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database insertion failed: " + err.message });
        }
        res.status(200).json({ success: true, insertId: result.insertId });
    });
});

// Add this to your server.js to handle the password update
app.put('/api/update-password', async (req, res) => {
    const { username, newPassword } = req.body;

    try {
        // Hash the new password before saving
        const hashedPw = await bcrypt.hash(newPassword, 10);
        
        // SQL query to update the specific user
        const sql = "UPDATE login SET Password = ? WHERE Username = ?";
        
        db.execute(sql, [hashedPw, username], (err, result) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error(err);
                return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error" });
            }
            // Check if the username actually existed in the table
            if (result.affectedRows === 0) {
                return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: "User not found" });
            }
            res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: "Password updated!" });
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Server error" });
    }
});
// Route to fetch all users with a non-null role
app.get('/api/get-users', (req, res) => {

    db.execute(sql, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Fetch error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Error fetching users" });
        }
        res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

    if (searchTerm) {
        const pattern = `%${searchTerm}%`;
        sql += ` WHERE 
            doctor_name LIKE ? OR 
            email_id LIKE ? OR 
            phone_no LIKE ? OR 
            id LIKE ?`;
        params = [pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern];
    }

    sql += " ORDER BY id DESC";

    db.query(sql, params, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error(err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error" });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-doctor', (req, res) => {
    const { id, doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification } = req.body;

    if (id) {
        // UPDATE existing doctor
        const query = "UPDATE doctor_details SET doctor_name = ?, email_id = ?, phone_no = ?, notification_required = ? WHERE id = ?";
        db.query(query, [doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification, id], (err, result) => {
            if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err });
            res.json({ success: true, message: "Updated successfully" });
        });
    } else {
        // INSERT new doctor
        const query = "INSERT INTO doctor_details (doctor_name, email_id, phone_no, notification_required) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)";
        db.query(query, [doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification], (err, result) => {
            if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err });
            res.json({ success: true, message: "Added successfully" });
        });
    }
});

app.post('/api/add-doctor', (req, res) => {
    const { id, doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification } = req.body;

    let query;
    let queryParams;

    if (id) {
        query = "UPDATE doctor_details SET doctor_name = ?, email_id = ?, phone_no = ?, notification_required = ? WHERE id = ?";
        queryParams = [doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification, id];
    } else {
        query = "INSERT INTO doctor_details (doctor_name, email_id, phone_no, notification_required) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)";
        queryParams = [doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification];
    }

    db.query(query, queryParams, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("DB Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err });
        }

        // Send Email if notification is 'Yes'
        if (notification === 'Yes' && emailId) {
            console.log(`Attempting to send email to: ${emailId}`);
            
            const mailOptions = {
                from: `"Patho Consult Diagnostics" <dhanwanthiresathish2005@gmail.com>`,
                to: emailId,
                subject: `Registration Successful - Dr. ${doctorName}`,
                html: `
                    <div style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif; border: 1px solid #4a148c; padding: 20px; border-radius: 10px;">
                        <h2 style="color: #4a148c;">Welcome to Patho Consult</h2>
                        <p>Hello <strong>Dr. ${doctorName}</strong>,</p>
                        <p>You have been successfully registered in our diagnostic management system.</p>
                        <hr />
                        <p><strong>Registered Email:</strong> ${emailId}</p>
                        <p><strong>Contact Number:</strong> ${phoneNo}</p>
                        <br/>
                        <p>Regards,<br/><strong>Patho Consult Admin Team</strong></p>
                    </div>
                `
            };

            transporter.sendMail(mailOptions, (mailErr, info) => {
                if (mailErr) {
                    console.error("Mail Delivery Error:", mailErr);
                } else {
                    console.log("Email sent successfully: " + info.response);
                }
            });
        }

        res.json({ success: true, message: id ? "Updated" : "Added" });
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-client-code', (req, res) => {
    const { id, location, clientName, code, emailId, phoneNo, panNo, address, notification } = req.body;
    let sql = "";
    let params = [];

    if (id) {
        // UPDATE Logic
        sql = `UPDATE client_codes SET 
               location=?, client_name=?, client_code=?, email_id=?, 
               phone_no=?, pan_no=?, address=?, notification_required=? 
               WHERE id = ?`;
        params = [location, clientName, code, emailId, phoneNo, panNo, address, notification, id];
    } else {
        // INSERT Logic
        sql = `INSERT INTO client_codes 
               (location, client_name, client_code, email_id, phone_no, pan_no, address, notification_required) 
               VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)`;
        params = [location, clientName, code, emailId, phoneNo, panNo, address, notification];
    }

    // Execute Database Query
    db.query(sql, params, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("DB Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Database error" });
        }

        // --- EMAIL LOGIC STARTS HERE ---
        // We only send mail if notification is 'Yes' AND we have an email address
        if (notification === 'Yes' && emailId) {
            const mailOptions = {
                from: `"Patho Consult Diagnostics" <${process.env.EMAIL_USER}>`,
                to: emailId,
                subject: `Welcome ${clientName} - Client Registration Successful`,
                html: `
                    <div style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif; border: 1px solid #ddd; padding: 20px;">
                        <h2 style="color: #4a148c;">Welcome to Our System!</h2>
                        <p>Hello <strong>${clientName}</strong>,</p>
                        <p>Your client registration has been successfully processed.</p>
                        <table style="width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse;">
                            <tr><td style="padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #eee;"><strong>Client Code:</strong></td><td style="padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #eee;">${code}</td></tr>
                            <tr><td style="padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #eee;"><strong>Location:</strong></td><td style="padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #eee;">${location}</td></tr>
                        </table>
                        <p>Please find the attached welcome guide for more details.</p>
                        <br/>
                        <p>Best Regards,<br/>Admin Team</p>
                    </div>
                `,
                attachments: [
    {
        filename: 'WelcomeGuide.pdf',
        path: path.join(__dirname, 'files', 'WelcomeGuide.pdf') 
    }
]
            };

            transporter.sendMail(mailOptions, (error, info) => {
                if (error) {
                    console.log("Email failed to send:", error);
                } else {
                    console.log("Email sent successfully: " + info.response);
                }
            });
        }

        res.json({ 
            success: true, 
            message: id ? "Updated successfully" : "Added successfully" 
        });
    });
});

app.get('/api/clients/filter', (req, res) => {
    const searchTerm = req.query.search;

    let sql = "SELECT * FROM client_codes";
    let params = [];

    if (searchTerm) {
        const pattern = `%${searchTerm}%`;
        sql += ` WHERE 
            client_name LIKE ? OR 
            client_code LIKE ? OR 
            email_id LIKE ? OR 
            phone_no LIKE ? OR 
            pan_no LIKE ? OR 
            notification_required LIKE ? OR
            address LIKE ? OR 
            location LIKE ? OR
            id LIKE ?`;
        
        // There are 9 question marks above, so we provide the pattern 9 times
        params = [pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern];
    }

    sql += " ORDER BY id DESC";

    // Use db.query (or db.execute) with the params array
    db.query(sql, params, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("SQL Error Detail:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error" });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

app.get('/api/registration-metadata', (req, res) => {
    const titlesQuery = "SELECT id, title_name FROM titles";
    const doctorsQuery = "SELECT id, doctor_name FROM doctor_details"; 

    db.query(titlesQuery, (err, titleResults) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json(err);
        db.query(doctorsQuery, (err, doctorResults) => {
            if (err) return res.status(500).json(err);
            res.json({ 
                titles: titleResults, 
                doctors: doctorResults 
            });
        });
    });
});


app.get('/api/get-all-patients', (req, res) => {
    const sql = `
        SELECT 
            p.PatientID, 
            p.patient_name, 
            p.age, 
            p.gender, 
            p.phone_no, 
            d.doctor_name 
        FROM patients p
        LEFT JOIN doctor_details d ON p.doctor_id = d.id
        ORDER BY p.PatientID DESC
    `;

    db.query(sql, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Database Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Database fetch failed" });
        }
        res.json(results); 
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-patient', (req, res) => {
    // Added 'email' and 'dob'
    const { title_id, patient_name, age, gender, phone_no, doctor_id, email, dob } = req.body;
    
    // Validation: Ensure mandatory fields are present
    if (!title_id || !patient_name) {
        return res.status(400).json({ 
            success: false, 
            error: "Please fill all required fields (Title and Name)." 
        });
    }

    const sql = `INSERT INTO patients 
        (title_id, patient_name, age, gender, phone_no, doctor_id, email, dob) 
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)`;
    
    const values = [title_id, patient_name, age, gender, phone_no, doctor_id || null, email, dob];

    db.query(sql, values, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("DB Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ 
                success: false, 
                error: "Database save failed: " + err.sqlMessage 
            });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, message: "Patient registered successfully!", patientId: result.insertId });
    });
});
app.post('/api/register-patient', (req, res) => {
    const d = req.body; 

    // 1. Added GroupID to the column list
    const sql = `INSERT INTO patients (
        title_id, patient_name, age, gender, phone_no, email, dob, RegDate, external_id,
        door_no, flat_name, street_name1, street_name2, city, state, pincode, country,
        phone_home, locality, marital_status, notify_sms, notify_email, 
        group_name, social_relationship, social_name, employment_status, employer_name, 
        income_group, GroupID
    ) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)`;

    const values = [
        d.title_id, d.patient_name, d.age, d.gender, d.phone_no, d.email, d.dob || null, d.reg_date, d.group_client_code,
        d.door_no, d.flat_name, d.street_name1, d.street_name2, d.city, d.state, d.pincode, d.country,
        d.phone_home, d.locality, d.marital_status, d.notify_sms ? 1 : 0, d.notify_email ? 1 : 0,
        d.group_name, d.social_relationship, d.social_name, d.employment_status, d.employer_name, 
        d.income_group, 
        d.GroupID || null // 2. If no GroupID is provided, it registers as a standalone patient
    ];

    db.query(sql, values, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Save Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.sqlMessage });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, message: "Record Saved!", id: result.insertId });
    });
});
//customercare
app.get('/api/customer-view-full', (req, res) => {
    const { fromDate, toDate } = req.query;
    const sql = `
        SELECT 
            p.patient_name, 
            'Pending' AS lab_status, 
            'Paid' AS status,              -- Fixed: removed p.payment_status
            p.PatientID, 
            p.external_id, 
            p.client_code, 
            p.sample_id, 
            IFNULL(d.doctor_name, 'Self') AS referred_by, 
            IFNULL(ca.name, 'Main Center') AS collected_at, 
            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID) AS total_test_billed,
            0 AS test_saved,
            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID AND Status = 'Confirmed') AS confirmed_test,
            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID AND Status = 'Approved') AS approved_test,
            ((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID) - 
             (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID AND Status = 'Approved')) AS test_pending_approval,
            CONCAT('INV-', p.PatientID) AS invoice_no, 
            DATE_FORMAT(p.RegDate, '%d-%m-%Y %H:%i') AS invoice_date, 
            p.last_print_date,
            IFNULL(p.print_count, 0) AS total_print_count,
            p.email_sent_date,
            IFNULL(p.email_count, 0) AS total_emails_sent,
            'No' AS test_completed
        FROM patients p
        LEFT JOIN doctor_details d ON p.doctor_id = d.id
        LEFT JOIN collected_at ca ON p.PatientID = ca.id -- Updated to match your current data structure
        WHERE p.RegDate BETWEEN ? AND ?
    `;

    db.query(sql, [`${fromDate} 00:00:00`, `${toDate} 23:59:59`], (err, results) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.message });
        res.json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

app.post('/api/send-report-mail', async (req, res) => {
    const { email, sampleId, patientName, reportData } = req.body;

    // 1. Construct the HTML Template (Matching your Generate Report style)
    const htmlTemplate = `
    <html>
        <body style="font-family: sans-serif; padding: 30px;">
            <div style="border-bottom: 2px solid purple; margin-bottom: 20px;">
                <h1 style="color: purple; margin: 0;">Patho Consult</h1>
                <p>Mylapore, Chennai | Phone: 044-24934435</p>
            </div>
            <table style="width: 100%; margin-bottom: 30px; font-size: 14px;">
                <tr>
                    <td><strong>Name:</strong> ${patientName}</td>
                    <td><strong>Sample ID:</strong> ${sampleId}</td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                    <td><strong>Patient ID:</strong> ${reportData.PatientID || 'N/A'}</td>
                    <td><strong>Date:</strong> ${new Date().toLocaleDateString()}</td>
                </tr>
            </table>
            <div style="margin-top: 40px;">
                <h3>Test: Culture and Sensitivity</h3>
                <p><strong>Result:</strong> No significant pathogen grown in culture.</p>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top: 100px; border-top: 1px solid #ccc; padding-top: 10px;">
                <p>This is a computer-generated report and does not require a physical signature.</p>
            </div>
        </body>
    </html>`;

    // 2. Generate PDF and Send Email
    pdf.create(htmlTemplate, { format: 'A4' }).toBuffer(async (err, buffer) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("PDF Buffer Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Failed to generate PDF attachment" });
        }

        try {
            await transporter.sendMail({
                from: '"Patho Consult" <dhanwanthiresathish2005@gmail.com>',
                to: email,
                subject: `Diagnostic Report - ${patientName} (${sampleId})`,
                text: `Dear Sir/Madam,\n\nPlease find attached the diagnostic report for ${patientName}.\n\nRegards,\nPatho Consult Team`,
                attachments: [
                    {
                        filename: `Report_${sampleId}.pdf`,
                        content: buffer
                    }
                ]
            });

            res.json({ success: true });
        } catch (mailErr) {
            console.error("Nodemailer Error:", mailErr);
            res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: mailErr.message });
        }
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-test', (req, res) => {
    const d = req.body;

    // 1. Get the next ID from the database metadata to create a unique TestCode
    const getNextIdSql = "SELECT AUTO_INCREMENT FROM information_schema.TABLES WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = 'myapp_db' AND TABLE_NAME = 'Tests'";

    db.query(getNextIdSql, (err, data) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Metadata Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Could not generate Test Code" });
        }

        const nextId = data[0].AUTO_INCREMENT;
        // Generate a code, e.g., TST-1001, TST-1002...
        const generatedCode = `TST-${1000 + nextId}`;

        // 2. Updated SQL to include 'TestCode'
        const sql = `INSERT INTO Tests (
            measurementType, commonParagraph, culture, alternativeSample, 
            multipleComponents, calculationPresent, tableRequired, ageWiseCritical, 
            ageWiseReference, pregnancyReference, biopsyNumber, outsourced, 
            TestName, TestCode, CultureCategory, Department, SampleContainer, 
            Methodology, InstrumentReagent, Units, TurnAroundTime, 
            Price, ValidDate, TestSchedule, CutOffTime, 
            PatientPreparation, ExpectedResultDate, AdditionalComments, 
            TestInformation, SelectedProfile
        ) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)`;

        // 3. Insert 'generatedCode' into the values array
        const values = [
            d.measurementType, d.commonParagraph, d.culture, d.alternativeSample,
            d.multipleComponents, d.calculationPresent, d.tableRequired, d.ageWiseCritical,
            d.ageWiseReference, d.pregnancyReference, d.biopsyNumber, d.outsourced,
            d.testName, 
            generatedCode, // <--- NEW AUTO-GENERATED CODE
            d.cultureCategory, d.department, d.sampleContainer,
            d.methodology, d.instrumentReagent, d.units, d.turnAroundTime,
            d.amount || 0, d.validDate || null, d.testSchedule, d.cutOffTime || null,
            d.patientPreparation, d.expectedResultDate, d.additionalComments,
            d.testInformation, d.selectedProfile
        ];

        db.query(sql, values, (err, result) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error("Database Error:", err);
                return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.sqlMessage });
            }
            res.status(200).json({ 
                success: true, 
                message: `Test added successfully! Code generated: ${generatedCode}`,
                testCode: generatedCode 
            });
        });
    });
});

// --- 1. REGISTER PROFILE ---
app.post('/api/create-profile', async (req, res) => {
    const { profileName, displayName, amount } = req.body;
    
    try {
        const profileCode = "PR" + Math.floor(1000 + Math.random() * 9000);
        const query = "INSERT INTO profiles (profile_code, profile_name, display_name, amount) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)";
        
        // Using .promise() is the key to stopping the error you saw
        await db.promise().query(query, [profileCode, profileName, displayName, amount]);
        
        res.status(200).send({ message: "Profile registered successfully!", code: profileCode });
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Database Error:", err);
        res.status(500).send({ error: "Failed to save profile to database." });
    }
});

// --- 2. LINK SUB-PROFILE TO PROFILE ---
app.post('/api/link-subprofile', async (req, res) => {
    const { parentId, childId } = req.body;

    try {
        const query = "INSERT INTO profile_subprofile_mapping (parent_profile_id, child_profile_id) VALUES (?, ?)";
        
        await db.promise().query(query, [parentId, childId]);
        
        res.status(200).send({ message: "Sub-profile linked successfully!" });
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Linking error:", err);
        // Better error message for the user
        if (err.code === 'ER_DUP_ENTRY') {
            return res.status(400).send({ error: "This link already exists!" });
        }
        res.status(500).send({ error: "Database error. Please check server logs." });
    }
});

app.put('/api/update-profile/:id', (req, res) => {
    const { id } = req.params;
    const { amount, priority } = req.body;

    let updates = [];
    let params = [];

    // Check if amount is not null and not undefined (allows "0")
    if (amount !== null && amount !== undefined && amount !== "") {
        updates.push("amount = ?");
        params.push(amount);
    }

    // Check if priority is not null and not undefined (allows "0")
    if (priority !== null && priority !== undefined && priority !== "") {
        updates.push("priority = ?");
        params.push(priority);
    }

    if (updates.length === 0) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: "No fields provided for update" });
    }

    const query = `UPDATE profiles SET ${updates.join(", ")} WHERE id = ?`;
    params.push(id);

    db.query(query, params, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("DB Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
        }
        res.json({ message: "Updated successfully" });
    });
});

    }

app.get('/api/get-profile-details/:id', async (req, res) => {
    const { id } = req.params;

    try {
        // Fetch linked Tests with their specific mapping priority
        const testsQuery = `
            SELECT m.mapping_id AS link_id, t.TestID AS test_code, t.TestName AS test_name, m.priority 
            FROM profiletestmapping m
            JOIN tests t ON m.test_id = t.TestID
            WHERE m.profile_id = ?
            ORDER BY m.priority ASC`;

        // Fetch linked Sub-Profiles with their specific mapping priority
       const subProfilesQuery = `
    SELECT m.child_profile_id AS link_id, p.profile_code, p.profile_name, m.priority 
    FROM profile_subprofile_mapping m
    JOIN profiles p ON m.child_profile_id = p.id
    WHERE m.parent_profile_id = ?
    ORDER BY m.priority ASC`;

        const [tests] = await db.promise().query(testsQuery, [id]);
        const [subProfiles] = await db.promise().query(subProfilesQuery, [id]);

        res.json({ tests, subProfiles });
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Fetch Error:", err);
        res.status(500).send({ error: "Check if priority/id columns exist in mapping tables." });
    }
});
// Server.js - Update this section
app.put('/api/update-link-priority', async (req, res) => {
    const { linkId, priority, type, parentId } = req.body;
    
    try {
        if (type === 'test') {
            const query = `UPDATE profiletestmapping SET priority = ? WHERE mapping_id = ?`;
            await db.promise().query(query, [priority, linkId]);
        } else {
            // FIX: Ensure this query matches your table structure
            const query = `UPDATE profile_subprofile_mapping SET priority = ? 
                           WHERE parent_profile_id = ? AND child_profile_id = ?`;
            await db.promise().query(query, [priority, parentId, linkId]);
        }
        res.status(200).send({ message: "Updated" });
    } catch (err) {
        console.error(err);
        res.status(500).send(err);
    }
});
app.post('/api/link-test-to-profile', async (req, res) => {
    const { profileId, testId } = req.body;
    try {
        const query = "INSERT INTO profiletestmapping (profile_id, test_id, priority) VALUES (?, ?, 0)";
        await db.promise().query(query, [profileId, testId]);
        res.status(200).send({ message: "Test linked successfully!" });
    } catch (err) {
        if (err.code === 'ER_DUP_ENTRY') return res.status(400).send({ error: "Test already in profile!" });
        res.status(500).send(err);
    }
});
app.get('/api/test-elements', (req, res) => {
    // JOIN TestElements with Tests to get the parent metadata
    const sql = `
        SELECT 
            te.ElementID, 
            te.ElementName, 
            te.TestCode as ElementCode, 
            te.Priority, 
            t.TestName as ParentName, 
            t.Category as ParentCategory, 
            t.multipleComponents
        FROM TestElements te
        JOIN Tests t ON te.ParentTestID = t.TestID
        ORDER BY te.Priority ASC, te.ElementID DESC`;

    db.query(sql, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Fetch Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ message: "Database fetch failed" });
        }

        const responseData = results.map(el => ({
            id: el.ElementID, 
            element_name: el.ElementName,
            test_code: el.ElementCode || el.ParentCategory || `TID-${el.ElementID}`,
            test_name: el.ParentName, // This populates the "Test Name" display in your teal boxes
            existing_priority: el.Priority || 0,
            priority: el.Priority || 0,
            // Logic to separate into Multiple vs Single boxes
            category: el.multipleComponents === 'Yes' ? 'multiple' : 'single'
        }));
        
        res.status(200).json(responseData);
    });
});
app.post('/api/elements/add', (req, res) => {
    const { parentTestId, code, elementName } = req.body;

    // 1. Insert the child element linked to the ParentTestID
    const sql = `INSERT INTO TestElements (ParentTestID, ElementName, TestCode, IsActive) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)`;
    
    db.query(sql, [parentTestId, elementName, code, 1], (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.sqlMessage });
        }

        // 2. Automatically update parent to 'Yes' for multipleComponents
        const updateParentSql = "UPDATE Tests SET multipleComponents = 'Yes' WHERE TestID = ?";
        db.query(updateParentSql, [parentTestId]);

        res.status(201).json({ success: true, message: "Saved successfully!" });
    });
});

app.put('/api/elements/update-priority/:id', (req, res) => {
    let elementId = req.params.id;
    if (elementId.includes(':')) {
        elementId = elementId.split(':')[0];
    }

    const priority = parseInt(req.body.priority);

    // FIX: Changed 'id' to 'ElementID' to match your table schema
    const sql = "UPDATE TestElements SET Priority = ? WHERE ElementID = ?";
    
    db.query(sql, [priority, elementId], (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("SQL Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error: " + err.sqlMessage });
        }
        
        if (result.affectedRows === 0) {
            return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: "Element not found" });
        }

        res.json({ success: true, message: "Updated!" });
    });
});

//editratecard

app.post('/api/rates/update', (req, res) => {
    // These come from your EditRateCard.js formData
    const { profileName, amount, endDate, email, phone } = req.body;

    // 1. Update the 'profiles' table (Targeting your MariaDB schema)
    // We use profile_name to find the record and update the amount column
    const updateProfileSql = "UPDATE profiles SET amount = ? WHERE profile_name = ?";
    
    db.query(updateProfileSql, [amount, profileName], (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Profile Update Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Failed to update profile amount" });
        }

        // 2. Insert or Update the 'rates' history table
        // This keeps a log of WHO changed the rate and the expiry (EndDate)
        const updateRatesSql = `
            INSERT INTO rates (ProfileName, Rate, EndDate, CreatorEmail, CreatorPhone) 
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE 
            Rate = VALUES(Rate), 
            EndDate = VALUES(EndDate), 
            CreatorEmail = VALUES(CreatorEmail), 
            CreatorPhone = VALUES(CreatorPhone)`;

        db.query(updateRatesSql, [profileName, amount, endDate, email, phone], (err2, result2) => {
            if (err2) {
                console.error("Rates Table Error:", err2);
                return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Profile updated, but rate log failed." });
            }
            
            res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: "Profile rate and history log updated!" });
        });
    });
});
