//lab-view
// --- LAB VIEW DATA FETCHING ---
app.get('/api/lab-view-data', (req, res) => {
    const { fromDate, toDate } = req.query;

    const sql = `
        SELECT 
            p.patient_name, 
            p.PatientID AS patient_id, 
            p.external_id, 
            DATE_FORMAT(p.RegDate, '%d-%m-%Y %H:%i') AS collected_at,
            p.client_code, 
            'Pending' AS lab_status,             -- Default clinical status
            'Unpaid' AS status,                  -- Payment status placeholder
            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID) AS test_billed,
            0 AS test_saved,                     -- Placeholder for drafted tests
            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID AND Status = 'Confirmed') AS confirmed_test,
            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID AND Status = 'Approved') AS approved_test,
            ((SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID) - 
             (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM patient_billing_details WHERE PatientID = p.PatientID AND Status = 'Approved')) AS test_pending_approval,
            DATE_FORMAT(p.RegDate, '%d-%m-%Y') AS create_date,
            'No' AS test_completed,
            p.sample_id
        FROM patients p
        WHERE p.RegDate BETWEEN ? AND ?
        ORDER BY p.RegDate DESC
    `;

    const params = [`${fromDate} 00:00:00`, `${toDate} 23:59:59`];

    db.query(sql, params, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Lab View Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.sqlMessage });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

app.post('/api/save-test-template', (req, res) => {
    const { elementId, ranges } = req.body; 
    console.log("Received Payload:", req.body);

    if (!elementId || !ranges || !ranges.length) {
        return res.status(400).json({ 
            success: false, 
            message: `Missing data. Received elementId: ${elementId}` 
        });
    }
    const values = ranges.map(r => [
        elementId, 
        r.template_name || 'General', 
        r.lower_limit || null, 
        r.upper_limit || null, 
        r.unit || ''
    ]);

    const sql = `INSERT INTO test_element_templates 
                 (element_id, template_name, lower_limit, upper_limit, unit) 
                 VALUES ?`;

    db.query(sql, [values], (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Database Error:", err.sqlMessage);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.sqlMessage });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, message: "Template saved!" });
    });
});

app.get('/api/get-all-tests', (req, res) => {
    // Aliasing 'TestID' as 'id' ensures MUI DataGrid and other components 
    // find a unique identifier automatically.
    const sql = `
        SELECT 
            TestID AS id, 
            TestID, 
            TestName, 
            TestCode, 
            IFNULL(Price, 0) AS Price, 
            IFNULL(Price, 0) AS amount, 
            Department, 
            TestSchedule, 
            TurnAroundTime, 
            IsActive 
        FROM tests 
        ORDER BY TestName ASC`;

    db.query(sql, (err, results) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.message });
        res.json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

// Update Department Priorities
app.post('/api/update-dept-priority', (req, res) => {
    const { priorities } = req.body; // Expecting an array of { id, priority }

    if (!priorities || !Array.isArray(priorities)) {
        return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: "Invalid data format" });
    }

    // We use a Promise.all to ensure all updates complete
    const updatePromises = priorities.map(item => {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const sql = "UPDATE departments SET Priority = ? WHERE DepartmentID = ?";
            db.query(sql, [item.priority, item.id], (err, result) => {
                if (err) reject(err);
                else resolve(result);
            });
        });
    });

    Promise.all(updatePromises)
        .then(() => res.json({ success: true, message: "All priorities updated successfully!" }))
        .catch(err => {
            console.error(err);
            res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
        });
});

    });
});

    const updatePromises = priorities.map(item => {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const sql = "UPDATE tests SET Priority = ? WHERE TestID = ?";
            db.query(sql, [item.priority, item.id], (err, result) => {
                if (err) reject(err);
                else resolve(result);
            });
        });
    });

    Promise.all(updatePromises)
        .then(() => res.json({ success: true, message: "Test priorities updated!" }))
        .catch(err => res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message }));
});
// 1. Get unique categories for the dropdown
app.get('/api/get-test-categories', (req, res) => {
    const sql = "SELECT DISTINCT Category FROM tests WHERE Category IS NOT NULL ORDER BY Category ASC";
    db.query(sql, (err, result) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
        res.json({ success: true, data: result });
    });
});

// 2. Get tests by selected category
app.get('/api/get-tests-by-category', (req, res) => {
    const { category } = req.query;
    const sql = "SELECT TestID, TestName, TestCode, Priority FROM tests WHERE Category = ? ORDER BY TestName ASC";
    db.query(sql, [category], (err, result) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
        res.json({ success: true, data: result });
    });
});

// 3. Bulk Update Priorities
app.post('/api/update-test-priority', (req, res) => {
    const { priorities } = req.body; // Array of {id, priority}
    
    const queries = priorities.map(item => {
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const sql = "UPDATE tests SET Priority = ? WHERE TestID = ?";
            db.query(sql, [item.priority, item.id], (err, result) => {
                if (err) reject(err);
                else resolve(result);
            });
        });
    });

    Promise.all(queries)
        .then(() => res.json({ success: true }))
        .catch(err => res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message }));
});

// Fetch tests using the Department Name string
app.get('/api/get-tests-by-dept-name/:deptName', (req, res) => {
    const { deptName } = req.params;
    const sql = "SELECT TestID, TestName, TestCode, Priority FROM tests WHERE Department = ? ORDER BY TestName ASC";
    
    db.query(sql, [deptName], (err, result) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
        res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: result });
    });
});
// GET template by Test ID
app.get('/api/get-template/:testId', (req, res) => {
    const { testId } = req.params;
    const sql = "SELECT * FROM test_templates WHERE test_id = ?";
    
    db.query(sql, [testId], (err, result) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
        
        // Return the first match or null if not found
        res.status(200).json({ 
            success: true, 
            data: result.length > 0 ? result[0] : null 
        });
    });
});

app.post('/api/save-template', (req, res) => {
    const { testId, templateName, content } = req.body;

    // Use REPLACE INTO to update if it exists, or insert if it's new
    const sql = `INSERT INTO test_templates (test_id, template_name, test_content) 
                 VALUES (?, ?, ?) 
                 ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE test_content = VALUES(test_content)`;

    db.query(sql, [testId, templateName, content], (err, result) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
        res.json({ success: true, message: "Template saved successfully!" });
    });
});

app.put('/api/edit-isolated-organ/:id', (req, res) => {
    const { id } = req.params;
    const { organismName, cultureCategory } = req.body;

    // Update both fields in MariaDB
    const sql = `
        UPDATE isolated_organs 
        SET organism_name = ?, culture_category = ? 
        WHERE id = ?
    `;
    
    db.query(sql, [organismName, cultureCategory, id], (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error(err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error" });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, message: "Record updated successfully" });
    });
});

// server.js or routes/invoices.js

app.get('/api/invoices', (req, res) => {
    const { from, to } = req.query;

    // 1. The core query (as per your working terminal version)
    let sqlQuery = `
        SELECT 
            pb.id AS id, 
            CONCAT('INVPC', pb.id) AS invoiceNo, 
            DATE_FORMAT(p.RegDate, '%d-%m-%Y') AS date, 
            COALESCE(p.sample_id, 'N/A') AS sampleId, 
            p.PatientID AS patientId, 
            p.patient_name AS patientName, 
            pb.Amount AS totalAmount, 
            pb.Status AS invoiceStatus,
            p.client_code AS clientCode,
            COALESCE(d.doctor_name, 'Self') AS referredBy
        FROM patient_billing_details pb
        LEFT JOIN patients p ON pb.PatientID = p.PatientID
        LEFT JOIN doctor_details d ON p.doctor_id = d.id
    `;

    let queryParams = [];

    // 2. Add filtering ONLY if 'from' and 'to' dates are provided
    if (from && to) {
        // We filter by p.RegDate because that's where the date lives
        sqlQuery += " WHERE p.RegDate BETWEEN ? AND ?";
        queryParams = [from, to];
    }

    // 3. Execute the query
    db.query(sqlQuery, queryParams, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Database Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to fetch invoices" });
        }
        res.json(results);
    });
});
app.post('/api/register-group', (req, res) => {
    const { group_name, group_amount, total_persons, client_code } = req.body;
    const sql = "INSERT INTO groups (GroupName, TotalAmount, NumPersons, ClientCode) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)";
    
    db.query(sql, [group_name, group_amount, total_persons, client_code], (err, result) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false });
        
        // This 'insertId' is the key to matching
        res.json({ success: true, groupId: result.insertId }); 
    });
});
app.get('/api/get-groups', (req, res) => {
    // Aliasing ensures the JSON keys match your React code exactly
    const sql = `SELECT 
                    GroupID AS GroupID, 
                    GroupName AS GroupName, 
                    TotalAmount AS TotalAmount, 
                    NumPersons AS NumPersons, 
                    ClientCode AS ClientCode 
                 FROM groups`;
    
    db.query(sql, (err, results) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).send(err);
        res.json(results);
    });
});

app.get('/api/get-group-count/:groupId', (req, res) => {
    const { groupId } = req.params;
    const query = 'SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM patients WHERE GroupID = ?';
    
    db.query(query, [groupId], (err, results) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json(err);
        res.json({ count: results[0].count });
    });
});

app.put('/api/tests/toggle-status/:id', (req, res) => {
    const { id } = req.params;
    const { status } = req.body; // status will be 0 or 1
    const sql = "UPDATE tests SET IsActive = ? WHERE TestID = ?";
    db.query(sql, [status, id], (err, result) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json(err);
        res.json({ success: true, message: "Status updated" });
    });
});

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useLocation, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

function PatientDetailScreen() {
    const location = useLocation();
    const navigate = useNavigate();
    const { patient } = location.state || {};

    // --- STATES ---
    const [locations, setLocations] = useState([]);
    const [clients, setClients] = useState([]);
    const [doctors, setDoctors] = useState([]);
    const [testList, setTestList] = useState([]);
    const [billingType, setBillingType] = useState('self');
    
    // State for Client Autofill
    const [selectedClientId, setSelectedClientId] = useState('');

    useEffect(() => {
        const loadAllData = async () => {
            try {
                // 1. Fetch Locations
                const locRes = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/get-locations');
                const locData = await locRes.json();
                setLocations(Array.isArray(locData) ? locData : locData.data || []);

                // 2. Fetch Clients (Used for Autofill)
const clientRes = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/get-clients');
const clientData = await clientRes.json();

// Fix: Extract the 'data' array from the response object
if (clientData.success && Array.isArray(clientData.data)) {
    setClients(clientData.data);
} else {
    setClients([]);
}

                // 3. Fetch Doctors (Nested in metadata object)
                const metaRes = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/registration-metadata');
                const metaData = await metaRes.json();
                setDoctors(metaData.doctors || []);

                // 4. Fetch Tests
                const testRes = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/get-lab-tests');
                const testData = await testRes.json();
                setTestList(Array.isArray(testData) ? testData : testData.data || []);

            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Data loading failed:", error);
            }
        };

        loadAllData();
    }, []);

    if (!patient) return (
        <div style={{ padding: '50px', textAlign: 'center', color: '#4a148c' }}>
            <h2>No Patient Context Found</h2>
            <button onClick={() => navigate('/frontdesk')} style={styles.submitBtn}>Return to Home</button>
        </div>
    );

    return (
        <div style={styles.container}>
            {/* --- TOP HEADER --- */}
            <div style={styles.topHeader}>
                <div style={styles.headerLeft}>
                    <div style={styles.breadcrumb}>
                        Front Desk / <span style={{color: '#fff', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>Workflow</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.logoSection}>
                    <div style={styles.pulseDot}></div>
                    <span style={styles.logoText}>PATHO <span style={{fontWeight: '300'}}>CONSULT</span></span>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.headerRight}>
                    <span style={styles.systemStatus}>● System Live</span>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div style={{ display: 'flex', flex: 1, marginTop: '70px' }}>
                {/* LEFT SIDEBAR */}
                <div style={styles.sidebar}>
                    <div style={styles.avatarCircle}>
                        {patient.patient_name?.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}
                    </div>
                    <h3 style={styles.patientName}>{patient.patient_name}</h3>
                    <p style={styles.patientId}>ID: {patient.PatientID}</p>
                    
                    <div style={styles.infoGrid}>
                        <div style={styles.infoItem}>
                            <span style={styles.infoLabel}>AGE</span>
                            <span style={styles.infoValue}>{patient.age} Years</span>
                        </div>
                        <div style={styles.infoItem}>
                            <span style={styles.infoLabel}>GENDER</span>
                            <span style={styles.infoValue}>{patient.gender || 'Not Specified'}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div style={styles.infoItem}>
                            <span style={styles.infoLabel}>PHONE</span>
                            <span style={styles.infoValue}>{patient.phone_no || 'N/A'}</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <button onClick={() => navigate('/frontdesk')} style={styles.homeBtn}>
                        ← Back to Dashboard
                    </button>
                </div>

                {/* RIGHT MAIN CONTENT */}
                <div style={styles.mainContent}>
                    <div style={styles.tabContainer}>
                        {['self', 'insurance', 'out'].map((type) => (
                            <div 
                                key={type}
                                onClick={() => setBillingType(type)}
                                style={{
                                    ...styles.tab,
                                    ...(billingType === type ? styles.activeTab : {})
                                }}
                            >
                                {type === 'out' ? 'OUT OF HOSPITAL' : `${type.toUpperCase()} PAY`}
                            </div>
                        ))}
                    </div>

                    <div style={styles.formCard}>
                        <div style={styles.formGrid}>
                            {/* Branch Selection */}
                            <div style={styles.inputGroup}>
                                <label style={styles.label}>Location*</label>
                                <select style={styles.select}>
                                    <option value="">Select Branch</option>
                                    {locations.map(loc => (
                                        <option key={loc.id} value={loc.LocationCode}>{loc.LocationName}</option>
                                    ))}
                                </select>
                            </div>

                           {/* CLIENT AUTOFILL SECTION */}
{billingType === 'self' && (
    <div style={styles.inputGroup}>
        <label style={styles.label}>Client Code / Client Name*</label>
        <div style={{display: 'flex', gap: '8px'}}>
            <select 
                style={{...styles.input, width: '120px'}}
                value={selectedClientId}
                onChange={(e) => setSelectedClientId(e.target.value)}
            >
                <option value="">Code</option>
                {/* FIX: Use client_code instead of ClientCode */}
                {clients.map(c => (
                    <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.client_code}</option>
                ))}
            </select>
            <select 
                style={styles.select}
                value={selectedClientId}
                onChange={(e) => setSelectedClientId(e.target.value)}
            >
                <option value="">Select Client Name</option>
                {/* FIX: Use client_name instead of GroupName */}
                {clients.map(c => (
                    <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.client_name}</option>
                ))}
            </select>
        </div>
    </div>
)}

                            {/* Referral Doctor */}
                            <div style={styles.inputGroup}>
                                <label style={styles.label}>Referral Source / Doctor*</label>
                                <select style={styles.select}>
                                    <option value="">Select Doctor...</option>
                                    {doctors.map(doc => (
                                        <option key={doc.id} value={doc.id}>{doc.doctor_name}</option>
                                    ))}
                                </select>
                            </div>

                            {/* Test Selection */}
                            <div style={styles.inputGroup}>
                                <label style={styles.label}>Add Tests / Profiles*</label>
                                <div style={{display: 'flex', gap: '8px'}}>
                                    <select style={styles.select}>
                                        <option value="">Select Test or Profile...</option>
                                        {testList.map(test => (
                                            <option key={test.id} value={test.amount}>
                                                {test.profile_name} - ₹{test.amount}
                                            </option>
                                        ))}
                                    </select>
                                    <button style={styles.addBtn}>+</button>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        {/* BILLING SECTION */}
                        <div style={styles.paymentSection}>
                            <h4 style={styles.sectionTitle}>Billing Summary</h4>
                            <div style={styles.paymentModes}>
                                {['Cash', 'Card', 'UPI/Digital', 'Credit'].map(m => (
                                    <label key={m} style={styles.checkboxLabel}>
                                        <input type="checkbox" style={{accentColor: '#4a148c'}} /> {m}
                                    </label>
                                ))}
                            </div>
                            
                            <div style={styles.amountGrid}>
                                <div style={styles.amountBox}>
                                    <span>Total Amount</span>
                                    <input style={styles.amountInput} value="0.00" readOnly />
                                </div>
                                <div style={styles.amountBox}>
                                    <span style={{color: '#2e7d32', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>Amount Paid</span>
                                    <input style={{...styles.amountInput, borderColor: '#2e7d32'}} placeholder="0.00" />
                                </div>
                                <div style={styles.amountBox}>
                                    <span style={{color: '#d32f2f'}}>Due Balance</span>
                                    <input style={styles.amountInput} value="0.00" readOnly />
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <div style={styles.footer}>
                            <button style={styles.cancelBtn} onClick={() => setSelectedClientId('')}>Reset Form</button>
                            <button style={styles.submitBtn}>Generate Invoice →</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";

function FrontDesk() {
    // 1. Define states at the very top of the component
    // 2. Initialize navigate at the very top of the component
    const navigate = useNavigate();
    const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("Patient Registration");
    const [isGroupOpen, setIsGroupOpen] = useState(false);
    const [currentDateTime, setCurrentDateTime] = useState("");
    const [metadata, setMetadata] = useState({ titles: [], doctors: [] });
    const [patients, setPatients] = useState([]); 
    const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState("");
    const [category, setCategory] = useState(null); // 'self', 'insurance', or 'out'
    const STATUS_CONFIG = {
    Approved: { label: 'COMPLETED', color: '#2e7d32' },  // Green
    Pending: { label: 'DUE / PENDING', color: '#ef6c00' }, // Orange
    New: { label: 'REGISTERED', color: '#7b1fa2' }       // Purple
};
const [filterType, setFilterType] = useState("All"); // Options: "All", "Pending", "Approved"
   
    // --- 1. MODAL STATES ---
const [decisionModal, setDecisionModal] = useState({ 
    show: false, 
    title: '', 
    onConfirm: null, 
    onCancel: null 
});

const [successModal, setSuccessModal] = useState({ 
    show: false, 
    type: '', 
    message: '' 
});
    
    const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
        title_id: '',
        patient_name: '',
        gender: '',
        phone_no: '',
        email: '',
        age: '',
        dob: '',
        doctor_id: '',
        door_no: '',
    flat_name: '',
    street_name1: '',
    street_name2: '',
    state: '',
    city: '',
    pincode: '',
    country: '',
    phone_home: '',
    locality: '',
    marital_status: '',
    notify_sms: false,
    notify_email: false,
    group_name: '',
    group_amount: '',
    group_total_persons: '',
    group_to_be_registered: '',
    group_client_code: '',
    social_relationship: '',
    social_name: '',
    employment_status: '',
    employer_name: '',
    employer_address: '',
    social_city: '',
    social_pincode: '',
    social_state: '',
    income_group: '',
    external_id: '',   // The unique Patient Sequence (e.g., PAT-101)
    client_code: '',   // The Group/Corporate Code (e.g., CORP-001)
    GroupID: null
    });
    // --- Data Grid Logic ---
const [sortConfig, setSortConfig] = useState({ key: 'patient_name', direction: 'asc' });
const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1);
const [rowsPerPage] = useState(10);
const [columnFilters, setColumnFilters] = useState({ patient_name: '', PatientID: '', gender: '' });
const [payDueModal, setPayDueModal] = useState({ show: false, patient: null });
const [collectAmount, setCollectAmount] = useState("");

const [collectedAmount, setCollectedAmount] = useState("");
const [groupInvoiceModal, setGroupInvoiceModal] = useState({ show: false, patient: null });
const [groupPaymentModal, setGroupPaymentModal] = useState({ show: false, data: null });


// --- 1. FILTERING LOGIC (Must be first) ---
const filteredPatients = patients.filter(p => {
    // Top-level Global Search
    const matchesSearch = 
        p.patient_name.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()) ||
        p.PatientID.toString().includes(searchTerm) ||
        p.phone_no.includes(searchTerm);

    // Column-specific Header Filters (Name, ID, Gender)
    const matchesColumnFilters = 
        p.patient_name.toLowerCase().includes(columnFilters.patient_name.toLowerCase()) &&
        p.PatientID.toString().includes(columnFilters.PatientID) &&
        p.gender.toLowerCase().includes(columnFilters.gender.toLowerCase());

    // Status Tab logic (All / Pending / Approved)
    let matchesStatus = true;
    if (filterType === 'Pending') matchesStatus = p.current_status === 'Pending';
    if (filterType === 'Approved') matchesStatus = p.current_status === 'Approved';
    
    return matchesSearch && matchesColumnFilters && matchesStatus;
});

// --- 2. SORTING LOGIC (Must be second) ---
const sortedPatients = [...filteredPatients].sort((a, b) => {
    const aValue = a[sortConfig.key] || "";
    const bValue = b[sortConfig.key] || "";
    
    if (aValue < bValue) return sortConfig.direction === 'asc' ? -1 : 1;
    if (aValue > bValue) return sortConfig.direction === 'asc' ? 1 : -1;
    return 0;
});

// --- 3. PAGINATION LOGIC (Must be third) ---
const indexOfLastRow = currentPage * rowsPerPage;
const indexOfFirstRow = indexOfLastRow - rowsPerPage;
const currentRows = sortedPatients.slice(indexOfFirstRow, indexOfLastRow);
const totalPages = Math.ceil(sortedPatients.length / rowsPerPage);

// --- 4. HANDLER FUNCTIONS ---
const requestSort = (key) => {
    let direction = 'asc';
    if (sortConfig.key === key && sortConfig.direction === 'asc') direction = 'desc';
    setSortConfig({ key, direction });
};

const handleColumnFilter = (e, column) => {
    setColumnFilters({ 
        ...columnFilters, 
        [column]: e.target.value 
    });
    setCurrentPage(1); 
};

const handleFilterChange = (e, column) => {
    setColumnFilters({ ...columnFilters, [column]: e.target.value });
    setCurrentPage(1); // Reset to page 1 when filtering
};

    const fetchPatients = async () => {
      
    try {
        const res = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/get-all-patients');
        const data = await res.json();
        // Assuming you have a state called 'patients'
        // If not, add: const [patients, setPatients] = useState([]); at the top
        setPatients(data); 
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Error fetching patient list:", err);
    }
};
const handleSelectPatient = (patient) => {
    // Scroll to the top of the form so the user sees the populated data
    window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });

    // Set the form data state with the patient's existing records
    setFormData({
        ...formData, // Keep existing fields not present in the patient object
        PatientID: patient.PatientID, // Important: This triggers the "Cancel Edit" button
        patient_name: patient.patient_name,
        gender: patient.gender,
        phone_no: patient.phone_no,
        email: patient.email || '',
        age: patient.age,
        external_id: patient.external_id,
        GroupID: patient.GroupID,
        group_name: patient.group_name || '',
        // Include address and other metadata if they exist in your patient object
        door_no: patient.door_no || '',
        street_name1: patient.street_name1 || '',
        city: patient.city || '',
        state: patient.state || '',
        pincode: patient.pincode || '',
        marital_status: patient.marital_status || ''
    });

    // If the patient belongs to a group, ensure the group section is visible
    if (patient.GroupID) {
        setIsGroupOpen(true);
    }
};
// FrontDesk.js

const handleQuickPaySubmit = async () => {
    const patient = payDueModal.patient;
    const amountToCollect = parseFloat(collectedAmount);

    if (!amountToCollect || amountToCollect <= 0) {
        alert("Please enter a valid amount.");
        return;
    }

    try {
        const response = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/update-due', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                patientId: patient.PatientID,
                payAmount: amountToCollect
            })
        });

        const result = await response.json();

        if (result.success) {
            // 1. Close the modal
            setPayDueModal({ show: false, patient: null });
            setCollectedAmount("");

            // 2. REFRESH the patient list
            // This re-runs the SQL with SUM() logic, turning the badge Green
            fetchPatients(); 

            // 3. Show success notification
            setSuccessModal({
                show: true,
                message: `Payment of ₹${amountToCollect} received. Status updated to COMPLETED.`,
                type: 'success'
            });
        } else {
            alert("Error saving payment.");
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Payment Error:", error);
    }
};
useEffect(() => {
    fetchPatients();

    // 1. Fetch the Next Available External ID
    const fetchNextID = async () => {
        try {
            const res = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/next-external-id');
            const data = await res.json();
            setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, external_id: data.nextId }));
        } catch (err) {
            console.error("Error fetching Next ID:", err);
        }
    };
    fetchNextID()

    // 1. Fetch Metadata (Titles, Doctors)
    fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/registration-metadata')
        .then(res => res.json())
        .then(data => {
            setMetadata(prev => ({ 
                ...prev, 
                titles: data.titles || [], 
                doctors: data.doctors || [] 
            }));
        })
        .catch(err => console.error("Metadata error", err));

    // 2. Fetch Groups
    fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/get-groups')
        .then(res => res.json())
        .then(data => {
            console.log("Groups loaded from server:", data);
            setMetadata(prev => ({ 
                ...prev, 
                groups: Array.isArray(data) ? data : [] // Ensure it is always an array
            }));
        })
        .catch(err => console.error("Error fetching groups:", err));
    // 2. The Dynamic Clock (Updates State EVERY Second)
    const timer = setInterval(() => {
        const now = new Date();
        
        const year = now.getFullYear();
        const month = String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
        const day = String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        const hours = String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
        const minutes = String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
        const seconds = String(now.getSeconds()).padStart(2, '0');

        const formatted = `${year}-${month}-${day} ${hours}:${minutes}:${seconds}`;
        
        // UPDATE DISPLAY
        setCurrentDateTime(formatted);

        // UPDATE DATA (This makes it truly dynamic for the database)
        setFormData(prev => ({
            ...prev,
            reg_date: formatted
        }));

    }, 1000);

    return () => clearInterval(timer);
}, []);
// Inside FrontDesk.js

// 1. Fetch the ID on load
useEffect(() => {
    const getNewID = async () => {
        try {
            const res = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/next-external-id');
            const data = await res.json();
            setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, external_id: data.nextId }));
        } catch (err) {
            console.error("Error fetching External ID:", err);
        }
    };
    getNewID();
}, []); // Empty dependency array ensures this only runs once on mount

const isFormValid = () => {
    const requiredFields = [
        'title_id', 'patient_name', 'gender', 'phone_no', 'age', 
        'door_no', 'street_name1', 'city', 'state', 'pincode', 'marital_status'
    ];
    
    const missing = requiredFields.filter(field => !formData[field]);
    
    if (missing.length > 0) {
        alert(`Please fill all required fields: ${missing.join(', ')}`);
        return false;
    }
    return true;
};
    const tabs = ["Patient Registration", "Contact Details", "Social/Economic Information", "Emergency Contact"];

// --- 2. REGISTRATION WORKFLOW ---
const handleRegistrationWorkflow = () => {
    if (!validateForm()) return;

    // Step A: Ask about Group
    setDecisionModal({
        show: true,
        title: "Do you want to register this patient with a Group?",
        onConfirm: () => {
            setIsGroupOpen(true);
            setDecisionModal({ show: false });
            // Wait for DOM to render the group section before scrolling
            setTimeout(() => {
                const element = document.getElementById('group-section-container');
                if (element) element.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
            }, 100);
        },
        onCancel: () => {
            // Step B: If No, ask to submit as Individual
            setDecisionModal({
                show: true,
                title: "Submit as an individual patient?",
                onConfirm: () => {
                    setDecisionModal({ show: false });
                    handleRegister(); // Execute Individual Reg
                },
                onCancel: () => setDecisionModal({ show: false })
            });
        }
    });
};

// 2. Fix resetForm so it fetches a NEW ID for the next patient
const resetForm = async () => {
    // Clear all form fields to their initial state
    setFormData({
        title_id: '',
        patient_name: '',
        gender: '',
        phone_no: '',
        email: '',
        age: '',
        dob: '',
        doctor_id: '',
        door_no: '',
        flat_name: '',
        street_name1: '',
        street_name2: '',
        state: '',
        city: '',
        pincode: '',
        country: '',
        phone_home: '',
        locality: '',
        marital_status: '',
        notify_sms: false,
        notify_email: false,
        group_name: '',
        group_amount: '',
        group_total_persons: '',
        external_id: '', // Temporary clear
        client_code: '',
        GroupID: null
    });
    
    try {
        // Fetch the fresh ID for the next registration
        const res = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/next-external-id');
        const data = await res.json();
        setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, external_id: data.nextId }));
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Error fetching fresh ID during reset:", err);
    }
    
    setIsGroupOpen(false);
};

// 2. Updated Individual Registration Handler
const handleRegister = async () => {
    // Explicitly mapping to ensure database columns match frontend state
    const finalData = { 
        ...formData, 
        external_id: formData.external_id, 
        client_code: formData.client_code,
        GroupID: null, 
        group_name: '' 
    };

    try {
        const response = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/register-patient', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(finalData)
        });
        const res = await response.json();
        if (res.success) {
            setSuccessModal({
                show: true,
                type: 'individual',
                message: `✨ Registration Successful! Patient ${formData.patient_name} has been added.`
            });
            fetchPatients();
            resetForm(); // <--- Auto-clear fields
        }
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Individual Reg Error:", err);
    }
};

const handleGroupRegister = async () => {
    if (!validateForm()) return;

    try {
        let currentGroupId = formData.GroupID;

        // 1. Create New Group if it doesn't exist
        if (!currentGroupId) {
            const gRes = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/register-group', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    group_name: formData.group_name,
                    group_amount: formData.group_amount,
                    total_persons: formData.group_total_persons,
                    client_code: formData.client_code 
                })
            });
            const gData = await gRes.json();
            if (gData.success) currentGroupId = gData.groupId;
        }

        // 2. Link Patient to Group
        const finalData = { 
            ...formData, 
            external_id: formData.external_id, 
            client_code: formData.client_code, 
            GroupID: currentGroupId 
        };

        const pRes = await fetch('http://localhost:5000/api/register-patient', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify(finalData)
        });

        if (pRes.ok) {
            // 3. Open the Responsive Payment/Invoice Box for Group Patients
            setGroupPaymentModal({
                show: true,
                data: finalData
            });
            
            fetchPatients();
            await resetForm(); 
        }
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Group Reg Error:", err);
    }
};
const validateForm = () => {
    // Define all fields that MUST be filled
    const required = [
        'title_id', 'patient_name', 'gender', 'phone_no', 'age', 
        'door_no', 'street_name1', 'city', 'state', 'pincode', 'marital_status'
    ];
    
    const missing = required.filter(field => !formData[field]);
    
    if (missing.length > 0) {
        alert(`Required fields missing: ${missing.join(', ').replace(/_/g, ' ')}`);
        return false;
    }
    return true;
};
const handleGroupSelection = (groupId) => {
    if (!groupId) {
        setFormData(prev => ({
            ...prev,
            GroupID: null,
            group_name: '',
            group_amount: '',
            client_code: '',
            group_total_persons: ''
        }));
        return;
    }

    const selectedGroup = metadata.groups.find(g => g.GroupID === parseInt(groupId));

    if (selectedGroup) {
        setFormData(prev => ({
            ...prev,
            GroupID: selectedGroup.GroupID || selectedGroup.groupid,
            group_name: selectedGroup.GroupName || selectedGroup.group_name,
            group_amount: selectedGroup.TotalAmount || selectedGroup.totalamount,
            client_code: selectedGroup.ClientCode || selectedGroup.client_code,
            group_total_persons: selectedGroup.NumPersons || selectedGroup.numpersons
        }));
        
        handleAutoFillGroup(selectedGroup.GroupID);
    }
};

// 2. Logic to calculate remaining slots available in a Group
const handleAutoFillGroup = async (groupId) => {
    if (!groupId) return;

    try {
        // Fetch the current count from the server
        const res = await fetch(`http://localhost:5000/api/get-group-count/${groupId}`);
        const data = await res.json();
        const alreadyRegistered = data.count || 0;

        setFormData(prev => {
            const total = parseInt(prev.group_total_persons) || 0;
            const remaining = total - alreadyRegistered;

            return {
                ...prev,
                // Ensure we don't show negative numbers
                group_to_be_registered: remaining > 0 ? remaining : 0
            };
        });
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Error fetching group registration count:", err);
    }
};
const handleGlobalSearch = async () => {
    if (!searchTerm) {
        // If search is empty, fetch everyone
        fetchPatients(); 
        return;
    }
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`http://localhost:5000/api/search-patients?term=${encodeURIComponent(searchTerm)}`);
        const data = await res.json();
        setPatients(data);
    } catch (err) {
        console.error("Search error:", err);
    }
};
    // --- Unified Purple Theme Styles ---
    const s = {

    const renderTabContent = () => {
        switch (activeTab) {
           case "Patient Registration":
    return (

                    >

                    style={{ ...s.btnOutline, padding: '4px 12px', opacity: currentPage === 1 ? 0.5 : 1 }}
                > Previous </button>
                <span style={{ alignSelf: 'center', fontWeight: 'bold', fontSize: '12px', color: '#4a148c', padding: '0 10px' }}>
                    {currentPage} / {totalPages || 1}
                </span>
                <button 
                    disabled={currentPage >= totalPages}
                    onClick={() => setCurrentPage(p => p + 1)}
                    style={{ ...s.btnOutline, padding: '4px 12px', opacity: currentPage >= totalPages ? 0.5 : 1 }}
                > Next </button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</section>
            </main>

            <footer style={s.footer}>
                🏥 Patho Consult Management System | Contact: 044-24934435 | {new Date().getFullYear()}
            </footer>
            {/* --- SPECIALIZED DECISION MODAL --- */}
{decisionModal.show && (
    <div style={s.modalOverlay}>
        <div style={s.modalBox}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: '40px', marginBottom: '15px' }}>❓</div>
            <h3 style={{ color: '#4a148c', margin: '0 0 20px 0', fontSize: '18px' }}>{decisionModal.title}</h3>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '12px', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
                <button 
                    style={{ ...s.btnPurple, padding: '10px 25px' }} 
                    onClick={decisionModal.onConfirm}
                > Yes, Proceed </button>
                <button 
                    style={{ ...s.btnOutline, padding: '10px 25px' }} 
                    onClick={decisionModal.onCancel}
                > No, Cancel </button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
)}

{/* --- SPECIALIZED SUCCESS MODAL --- */}
{successModal.show && (
    <div style={s.modalOverlay}>
        <div style={{ 
            ...s.modalBox, 
            borderTop: `8px solid ${successModal.type === 'group' ? '#4a148c' : successModal.type === 'error' ? '#d32f2f' : '#2e7d32'}` 
        }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: '50px', marginBottom: '10px' }}>
                {successModal.type === 'group' ? '🚀' : successModal.type === 'error' ? '⚠️' : '✅'}
            </div>
            <h2 style={{ color: '#333', marginBottom: '10px' }}>
                {successModal.type === 'error' ? 'Notice' : 'Success!'}
            </h2>
            <p style={{ color: '#666', lineHeight: '1.6', marginBottom: '25px' }}>{successModal.message}</p>
            <button 
                style={{ ...s.btnPurple, width: '100%', padding: '12px' }} 
                onClick={() => setSuccessModal({ show: false, type: '', message: '' })}
            > Close </button>
        </div>
    </div>
)}
{payDueModal.show && (
    <div style={s.modalOverlay}>
        <div style={{ ...s.modalBox, borderTop: '8px solid #ef6c00', width: '450px', padding: '0' }}>
            {/* Header */}
            <div style={{ backgroundColor: '#ef6c00', color: 'white', padding: '15px', textAlign: 'center' }}>
                <h3 style={{ margin: 0 }}>Quick Payment Collection</h3>
            </div>

            <div style={{ padding: '20px' }}>
                {/* Patient Info Card */}
                <div style={{ backgroundColor: '#f9f9f9', padding: '15px', borderRadius: '8px', marginBottom: '20px', border: '1px solid #eee' }}>
                    <p style={{ margin: '0 0 8px 0', fontSize: '14px' }}>Patient: <strong>{payDueModal.patient?.patient_name}</strong></p>
                    
                    {/* NEW: Test Names & Payment Mode */}
                    <p style={{ margin: '0 0 8px 0', fontSize: '13px', color: '#555' }}>
                        📋 Tests: <strong>{payDueModal.patient?.test_names || 'General Consultation'}</strong>
                    </p>
                    <p style={{ margin: '0 0 8px 0', fontSize: '13px', color: '#555' }}>
                        💳 Prev. Mode: <strong>{payDueModal.patient?.payment_modes || 'Not Set'}</strong>
                    </p>
                </div>

                {/* Financial Summary Row - Updated with Correct Aliases */}
<div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: '20px', textAlign: 'center' }}>
    <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
        <span style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: '#777' }}>Paid</span>
        {/* Match SQL: total_paid */}
        <p style={{ margin: 0, fontWeight: 'bold', color: '#2e7d32' }}>₹{payDueModal.patient?.total_paid || 0}</p>
    </div>
    <div style={{ flex: 1, borderLeft: '1px solid #ddd', borderRight: '1px solid #ddd' }}>
        <span style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: '#777' }}>Total Bill</span>
        {/* Match SQL: total_bill */}
        <p style={{ margin: 0, fontWeight: 'bold' }}>₹{payDueModal.patient?.total_bill || 0}</p>
    </div>
    <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
        <span style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: '#d32f2f' }}>Balance</span>
        {/* Match SQL: current_balance */}
        <p style={{ margin: 0, fontWeight: 'bold', color: '#d32f2f' }}>₹{payDueModal.patient?.current_balance || 0}</p>
    </div>
</div>
                
                <label style={{ fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 'bold', display: 'block', marginBottom: '5px' }}>Amount to Collect:</label>
                <input 
                    type="number" 
                    placeholder="Enter Received Amount"
                    value={collectedAmount}
                    onChange={(e) => setCollectedAmount(e.target.value)}
                    autoFocus
                    style={{ 
                        width: '100%', padding: '12px', marginBottom: '20px', 
                        borderRadius: '4px', border: '2px solid #ef6c00', fontSize: '18px', fontWeight: 'bold', textAlign: 'center'
                    }}
                />

                <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '10px' }}>
                    <button style={{ ...s.btnPurple, backgroundColor: '#2e7d32', flex: 2 }} onClick={handleQuickPaySubmit}>Confirm Collection</button>
                    <button style={{ ...s.btnOutline, flex: 1 }} onClick={() => { setPayDueModal({ show: false, patient: null }); setCollectedAmount(""); }}>Cancel</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
)}
// --- RESPONSIVE MODAL JSX (Add this at the bottom of your return) ---
{groupInvoiceModal.show && (
    <div style={s.modalOverlay}>
        <div style={{
            backgroundColor: 'white',
            padding: '25px',
            borderRadius: '15px',
            width: '90%',        // Responsive width
            maxWidth: '500px',   // Desktop limit
            maxHeight: '80vh',
            overflowY: 'auto',   // Scrollable if content is long
            boxShadow: '0 10px 25px rgba(0,0,0,0.2)'
        }}>
            <h3 style={{ color: '#4a148c', borderBottom: '2px solid #f0f0f0', paddingBottom: '10px' }}>
                Group Billing: {groupInvoiceModal.patient.patient_name}
            </h3>
            
            {/* Payment & Invoice Fields Required for Table */}
            <div style={{ display: 'grid', gap: '15px', marginTop: '15px' }}>
                <div>
                    <label style={s.label}>Total Amount</label>
                    <input type="number" style={s.input} placeholder="Enter Total Fee" />
                </div>
                <div>
                    <label style={s.label}>Payment Mode</label>
                    <select style={s.input}>
                        <option>Cash</option>
                        <option>UPI</option>
                        <option>Credit</option>
                    </select>
                </div>
                {/* Add any other specific "all info" fields here */}
            </div>

            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '10px', marginTop: '25px' }}>
                <button style={{ ...s.btnPurple, flex: 1 }} onClick={() => {/* Handle Save Invoice */}}>Generate Invoice</button>
                <button style={{ ...s.btnOutline, flex: 1 }} onClick={() => setGroupInvoiceModal({show:false})}>Cancel</button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
)}
        </div>
    );
}

const pdf = require('html-pdf');

app.get('/api/generate-report/:sampleId', (req, res) => {
    const { sampleId } = req.params;

    // We use LEFT JOIN so if doctor/location is missing, the patient is still found
    const sql = `
        SELECT p.*, 
               IFNULL(d.doctor_name, 'Self') AS doctor_name, 
               IFNULL(ca.name, 'Main Center') AS collection_center
        FROM patients p
        LEFT JOIN doctor_details d ON p.doctor_id = d.id
        LEFT JOIN collected_at ca ON p.PatientID = ca.id 
        WHERE p.sample_id = ?
    `;

    db.query(sql, [sampleId], (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Database Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).send("Database Error");
        }
        
        // This is where your previous error was triggered
        if (results.length === 0) {
            return res.status(404).send(`Error: No patient found with Sample ID: ${sampleId}`);
        }
        
        const data = results[0];

        // HTML Template for the PDF
        const htmlTemplate = `
        <html>
            <body style="font-family: sans-serif; padding: 30px;">
                <div style="border-bottom: 2px solid purple; margin-bottom: 20px;">
                    <h1 style="color: purple; margin: 0;">Patho Consult</h1>
                    <p>Mylapore, Chennai | Phone: 044-24934435</p>
                </div>
                <table style="width: 100%; margin-bottom: 30px; font-size: 14px;">
                    <tr>
                        <td><strong>Name:</strong> ${data.patient_name}</td>
                        <td><strong>Age/Sex:</strong> ${data.age} / ${data.gender}</td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                        <td><strong>Patient ID:</strong> ${data.PatientID}</td>
                        <td><strong>Sample ID:</strong> ${data.sample_id}</td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr>
                        <td><strong>Referred By:</strong> ${data.doctor_name}</td>
                        <td><strong>Date:</strong> ${data.RegDate}</td>
                    </tr>
                </table>
                <div style="margin-top: 40px;">
                    <h3>Test: Culture and Sensitivity</h3>
                    <p><strong>Specimen:</strong> Pus</p>
                    <p><strong>Result:</strong> No significant pathogen grown in culture.</p>
                </div>
                <div style="margin-top: 100px;">
                    <p><strong>${data.doctor_name}</strong><br>MD, PhD.</p>
                </div>
            </body>
        </html>`;

        const options = { format: 'A4' };

        pdf.create(htmlTemplate, options).toStream((err, stream) => {
            if (err) return res.status(500).send(err);
            res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/pdf');
            res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', `inline; filename=${sampleId}.pdf`);
            stream.pipe(res);
        });
    });
});

// 3. AUTHENTICATION ROUTE
app.post('/api/authenticate', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password, pin } = req.body;
  const sql = "SELECT * FROM login WHERE Username = ?";
  
  db.execute(sql, [username], async (err, results) => {
    if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error" });
    if (results.length === 0) return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: "User not found" });

    const user = results[0];
    const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.Password);
    
    if (!passwordMatch) {
      return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: "Invalid password" });
    }

    if (user.Username.toLowerCase() === 'admin') {
      const pinMatch = await bcrypt.compare(String(pin), user.Pin);
      if (!pinMatch) return res.status(403).json({ success: false, message: "Invalid Admin PIN" });
    }

    res.status(200).json({ 
      success: true, 
      role: user.Role || user.Username,
      token: "session_token_" + Date.now() 
    });
  });
});

// 4. FULL REGISTRATION ROUTE (With Role & Signature)
app.post('/api/register-full', upload.single('signature'), async (req, res) => {
    const { username, password, role, isAdmin } = req.body;
    const signaturePath = req.file ? req.file.path : null;

    try {
        const hashedPw = await bcrypt.hash(password, saltRounds);
        // Defaulting empty values for phone/address/pin to satisfy existing DB constraints
        const sql = `INSERT INTO login 
            (Username, Password, Role, IsAdmin, SignaturePath, Phone, Address, Pin, ISActive) 
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, '', '', '', 1)`;
        
        db.execute(sql, [username, hashedPw, role, isAdmin, signaturePath], (err, result) => {
            if (err) {
                if (err.code === 'ER_DUP_ENTRY') return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: "Username exists." });
                return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database failure." });
            }
            res.status(200).json({ success: true });
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Encryption error." });
    }
});

        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.sqlMessage });
        
        // Log this to your Terminal to see exactly what is being sent to React
        console.log("Data sent to frontend:", results); 
        
        res.json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

app.delete('/api/delete-user/:id', (req, res) => {
    const userId = req.params.id;
    
    // Instead of DELETE, we UPDATE the active status
    const sql = "UPDATE login SET ISActive = 0 WHERE ID = ?"; 

    db.query(sql, [userId], (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Database Error:", err.sqlMessage);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.sqlMessage });
        }
        
        if (result.affectedRows === 0) {
            return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: "User not found." });
        }

        res.json({ success: true, message: "User deactivated successfully" });
    });
});

// New Pathologist Registration Route (Handling Login + User Profiles)
app.post('/api/register-pathologist', upload.single('signature'), async (req, res) => {
    const {
        userName, firstName, lastName, gender, dob, age,
        undergraduateDegree, postgraduateDegree, registrationNumber, 
        designationCategory, designationForReport
    } = req.body;

    const signaturePath = req.file ? req.file.path : null;

    // 2. Use a connection from the pool for a Transaction
    db.getConnection((err, connection) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "DB Connection Error" });

        connection.beginTransaction(async (err) => {
            try {
                // STEP A: Insert into 'login' table first
                const hashedPw = await bcrypt.hash("patho123", saltRounds); // Default password
                const loginSql = "INSERT INTO login (Username, Password, Role, ISActive) VALUES (?, ?, 'Pathologist', 1)";
                
                connection.query(loginSql, [userName, hashedPw], (err, loginResult) => {
                    if (err) {
                        return connection.rollback(() => {
                            connection.release();
                            const msg = err.code === 'ER_DUP_ENTRY' ? "Username already exists." : "Login table error.";
                            res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: msg });
                        });
                    }

                    const newUserId = loginResult.insertId; // This is the ID for user_profiles

                    // STEP B: Insert into 'user_profiles' table
                    const profileSql = `
                        INSERT INTO user_profiles 
                        (user_id, FirstName, LastName, designation, Gender, DOB, Age, 
                        UndergraduateDegree, PostgraduateDegree, RegistrationNumber, 
                        DesignationForReport, SignaturePath) 
                        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)`;

                    const profileValues = [
                        newUserId, firstName, lastName, designationCategory, gender, 
                        dob || null, age || null, undergraduateDegree, 
                        postgraduateDegree, registrationNumber, 
                        designationForReport, signaturePath
                    ];

                    connection.query(profileSql, profileValues, (err) => {
                        if (err) {
                            return connection.rollback(() => {
                                connection.release();
                                console.error("Profile Error:", err);
                                res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Error saving profile details." });
                            });
                        }

                        // STEP C: Commit both inserts
                        connection.commit((err) => {
                            if (err) return connection.rollback(() => { throw err; });
                            connection.release();
                            res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: "Pathologist registered successfully!" });
                        });
                    });
                });
            } catch (error) {
                connection.rollback(() => {
                    connection.release();
                    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Server processing error." });
                });
            }
        });
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-out-of-hospital', (req, res) => {
    // Destructure everything coming from React
    const { location, hospitalName, createDate, testProfile, amount } = req.body;

    console.log("Incoming Data:", { location, hospitalName, createDate, testProfile, amount });

    db.getConnection((err, connection) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "DB Connection Error" });

        connection.beginTransaction((err) => {
            if (err) { connection.release(); return res.status(500).json({ success: false }); }

            // STEP 1: Insert Hospital
            const sqlClient = "INSERT INTO out_of_hospital_clients (LocationCode, HospitalName, CreatedAt) VALUES (?, ?, ?)";
            connection.query(sqlClient, [location, hospitalName, createDate], (err, result) => {
                if (err) {
                    return connection.rollback(() => {
                        connection.release();
                        console.error("Client Insert Error:", err.sqlMessage);
                        res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.sqlMessage });
                    });
                }

                const clientId = result.insertId;
                
                // STEP 2: Insert Rates
                // We use || 0 to ensure the decimal column gets a number even if 'amount' is empty
                const finalAmount = amount || 0;
                const sqlRate = "INSERT INTO out_of_hospital_rates (client_id, TestProfileName, Amount) VALUES (?, ?, ?)";
                
                connection.query(sqlRate, [clientId, testProfile, finalAmount], (err) => {
                    if (err) {
                        return connection.rollback(() => {
                            connection.release();
                            console.error("Rates Insert Error:", err.sqlMessage);
                            // This will send the EXACT database error back to your browser alert
                            res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database Error: " + err.sqlMessage });
                        });
                    }

                    // STEP 3: Commit
                    connection.commit((err) => {
                        if (err) return connection.rollback(() => { throw err; });
                        connection.release();
                        res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: "Stored Successfully!" });
                    });
                });
            });
        });
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-group', (req, res) => {
    const { 
        groupName, numPersons, amount, location, 
        hospitalName, referredBy, clientCode, clientName, 
        sampleCollect, paymentMode, paidAmount, netAmount, 
        profileTest,
        // Match these to the keys you send from React handleSave
        acc_holder, acc_no, cheque_no, bank_name, trans_id, digital_mode, status 
    } = req.body;

    // Use the EXACT column names from your DESCRIBE groups; output
    const sql = `INSERT INTO groups 
        (GroupName, NumPersons, TotalAmount, ProfileTest, LocationCode, 
        HospitalName, ReferredBy, ClientCode, ClientName, SampleCollect, 
        PaymentMode, PaidAmount, NetAmount, 
        acc_holder, acc_no, cheque_no, bank_name, trans_id, digital_mode, status,
        CreatedAt) 
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NOW())`;

    const values = [
        groupName || null, 
        parseInt(numPersons) || 0, 
        parseFloat(amount) || 0, 
        profileTest || null,      // Put ProfileTest here to match SQL order
        location || null,         // LocationCode
        hospitalName || null, 
        referredBy || null, 
        clientCode || null, 
        clientName || null, 
        sampleCollect || 'No',
        paymentMode || null, 
        parseFloat(paidAmount) || 0, 
        parseFloat(netAmount) || 0,
        // Individual Columns matching the destructuring above
        acc_holder || null,
        acc_no || null,
        cheque_no || null,
        bank_name || null,
        trans_id || null,
        digital_mode || null,
        status || 'Pending'
    ];

    db.query(sql, values, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("MariaDB Error Details:", err.message); // This will tell us if columns still mismatch
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database insertion failed: " + err.message });
        }
        res.status(200).json({ success: true, insertId: result.insertId });
    });
});

// Add this to your server.js to handle the password update
app.put('/api/update-password', async (req, res) => {
    const { username, newPassword } = req.body;

    try {
        // Hash the new password before saving
        const hashedPw = await bcrypt.hash(newPassword, 10);
        
        // SQL query to update the specific user
        const sql = "UPDATE login SET Password = ? WHERE Username = ?";
        
        db.execute(sql, [hashedPw, username], (err, result) => {
            if (err) {
                console.error(err);
                return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error" });
            }
            // Check if the username actually existed in the table
            if (result.affectedRows === 0) {
                return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: "User not found" });
            }
            res.status(200).json({ success: true, message: "Password updated!" });
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Server error" });
    }
});

            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Error fetching users" });
        }
        res.status(200).json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

        sql += ` WHERE 
            doctor_name LIKE ? OR 
            email_id LIKE ? OR 
            phone_no LIKE ? OR 
            id LIKE ?`;
        params = [pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern];

    sql += " ORDER BY id DESC";

    db.query(sql, params, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error(err);

        res.json({ success: true, data: results });
    });
});

    const { id, doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification } = req.body;

    if (id) {
        // UPDATE existing doctor
        const query = "UPDATE doctor_details SET doctor_name = ?, email_id = ?, phone_no = ?, notification_required = ? WHERE id = ?";
        db.query(query, [doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification, id], (err, result) => {
            if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err });
            res.json({ success: true, message: "Updated successfully" });
        });
    } else {
        // INSERT new doctor
        const query = "INSERT INTO doctor_details (doctor_name, email_id, phone_no, notification_required) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)";
        db.query(query, [doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification], (err, result) => {
            if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err });
            res.json({ success: true, message: "Added successfully" });
        });
    }
});

app.post('/api/add-doctor', (req, res) => {
    const { id, doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification } = req.body;

    let query;
    let queryParams;

    if (id) {
        query = "UPDATE doctor_details SET doctor_name = ?, email_id = ?, phone_no = ?, notification_required = ? WHERE id = ?";
        queryParams = [doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification, id];
    } else {
        query = "INSERT INTO doctor_details (doctor_name, email_id, phone_no, notification_required) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)";
        queryParams = [doctorName, emailId, phoneNo, notification];
    }

    db.query(query, queryParams, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("DB Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err });
        }

        // Send Email if notification is 'Yes'
        if (notification === 'Yes' && emailId) {
            console.log(`Attempting to send email to: ${emailId}`);
            
            const mailOptions = {
                from: `"Patho Consult Diagnostics" <dhanwanthiresathish2005@gmail.com>`,
                to: emailId,
                subject: `Registration Successful - Dr. ${doctorName}`,
                html: `
                    <div style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif; border: 1px solid #4a148c; padding: 20px; border-radius: 10px;">
                        <h2 style="color: #4a148c;">Welcome to Patho Consult</h2>
                        <p>Hello <strong>Dr. ${doctorName}</strong>,</p>
                        <p>You have been successfully registered in our diagnostic management system.</p>
                        <hr />
                        <p><strong>Registered Email:</strong> ${emailId}</p>
                        <p><strong>Contact Number:</strong> ${phoneNo}</p>
                        <br/>
                        <p>Regards,<br/><strong>Patho Consult Admin Team</strong></p>
                    </div>
                `
            };

            transporter.sendMail(mailOptions, (mailErr, info) => {
                if (mailErr) {
                    console.error("Mail Delivery Error:", mailErr);
                } else {
                    console.log("Email sent successfully: " + info.response);
                }
            });
        }

        res.json({ success: true, message: id ? "Updated" : "Added" });
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-client-code', (req, res) => {
    const { id, location, clientName, code, emailId, phoneNo, panNo, address, notification } = req.body;
    let sql = "";
    let params = [];

    if (id) {
        // UPDATE Logic
        sql = `UPDATE client_codes SET 
               location=?, client_name=?, client_code=?, email_id=?, 
               phone_no=?, pan_no=?, address=?, notification_required=? 
               WHERE id = ?`;
        params = [location, clientName, code, emailId, phoneNo, panNo, address, notification, id];
    } else {
        // INSERT Logic
        sql = `INSERT INTO client_codes 
               (location, client_name, client_code, email_id, phone_no, pan_no, address, notification_required) 
               VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)`;
        params = [location, clientName, code, emailId, phoneNo, panNo, address, notification];
    }

    // Execute Database Query
    db.query(sql, params, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("DB Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Database error" });
        }

        // --- EMAIL LOGIC STARTS HERE ---
        // We only send mail if notification is 'Yes' AND we have an email address
        if (notification === 'Yes' && emailId) {
            const mailOptions = {
                from: `"Patho Consult Diagnostics" <${process.env.EMAIL_USER}>`,
                to: emailId,
                subject: `Welcome ${clientName} - Client Registration Successful`,
                html: `
                    <div style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif; border: 1px solid #ddd; padding: 20px;">
                        <h2 style="color: #4a148c;">Welcome to Our System!</h2>
                        <p>Hello <strong>${clientName}</strong>,</p>
                        <p>Your client registration has been successfully processed.</p>
                        <table style="width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse;">
                            <tr><td style="padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #eee;"><strong>Client Code:</strong></td><td style="padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #eee;">${code}</td></tr>
                            <tr><td style="padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #eee;"><strong>Location:</strong></td><td style="padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #eee;">${location}</td></tr>
                        </table>
                        <p>Please find the attached welcome guide for more details.</p>
                        <br/>
                        <p>Best Regards,<br/>Admin Team</p>
                    </div>
                `,
                attachments: [
    {
        filename: 'WelcomeGuide.pdf',
        path: path.join(__dirname, 'files', 'WelcomeGuide.pdf') 
    }
]
            };

            transporter.sendMail(mailOptions, (error, info) => {
                if (error) {
                    console.log("Email failed to send:", error);
                } else {
                    console.log("Email sent successfully: " + info.response);
                }
            });
        }

        res.json({ 
            success: true, 
            message: id ? "Updated successfully" : "Added successfully" 
        });
    });
});

            client_name LIKE ? OR 
            client_code LIKE ? OR 
            email_id LIKE ? OR 
            phone_no LIKE ? OR 
            pan_no LIKE ? OR 
            notification_required LIKE ? OR
            address LIKE ? OR 
            location LIKE ? OR
            id LIKE ?`;
        
        // There are 9 question marks above, so we provide the pattern 9 times
        params = [pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern, pattern];
    }

    sql += " ORDER BY id DESC";

    // Use db.query (or db.execute) with the params array
    db.query(sql, params, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("SQL Error Detail:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error" });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, data: results });

    const doctorsQuery = "SELECT id, doctor_name FROM doctor_details"; 

    db.query(titlesQuery, (err, titleResults) => {

        db.query(doctorsQuery, (err, doctorResults) => {
            if (err) return res.status(500).json(err);
            res.json({ 
                titles: titleResults, 
                doctors: doctorResults 
            });
        });
    });
});


app.get('/api/get-all-patients', (req, res) => {
    const sql = `
        SELECT 
            p.*, 
            d.doctor_name,
            -- Get Status and Balance from the LATEST record for each patient
            COALESCE(b.Status, 'New') AS current_status,
            COALESCE(b.balance, 0) AS current_balance,
            GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT t.TestName SEPARATOR ', ') AS test_names
        FROM patients p
        LEFT JOIN doctor_details d ON p.doctor_id = d.id
        LEFT JOIN (
            SELECT pb1.* FROM patient_billing_details pb1
            WHERE pb1.id = (SELECT MAX(id) FROM patient_billing_details pb2 WHERE pb2.PatientID = pb1.PatientID)
        ) b ON p.PatientID = b.PatientID
        LEFT JOIN tests t ON b.TestID = t.TestID
        GROUP BY p.PatientID
        ORDER BY p.PatientID DESC
    `;

    db.query(sql, (err, results) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Database Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Database fetch failed" });
        }
        res.json(results); 
    });
});

app.post('/api/add-patient', (req, res) => {
    // Added 'email' and 'dob'

    // Validation: Ensure mandatory fields are present
    if (!title_id || !patient_name) {
        return res.status(400).json({ 
            success: false, 
            error: "Please fill all required fields (Title and Name)." 
        });
    }

    const sql = `INSERT INTO patients 
        (title_id, patient_name, age, gender, phone_no, doctor_id, email, dob) 
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)`;
    
    const values = [title_id, patient_name, age, gender, phone_no, doctor_id || null, email, dob];

    db.query(sql, values, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("DB Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ 
                success: false, 
                error: "Database save failed: " + err.sqlMessage 
            });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, message: "Patient registered successfully!", patientId: result.insertId });
    });
});
app.post('/api/register-patient', (req, res) => {
    const d = req.body; 

    // Updated SQL to include both external_id and client_code
    const sql = `INSERT INTO patients (
        title_id, patient_name, age, gender, phone_no, email, dob, RegDate, 
        external_id, client_code,
        door_no, flat_name, street_name1, street_name2, city, state, pincode, country,
        phone_home, locality, marital_status, notify_sms, notify_email, 
        group_name, social_relationship, social_name, employment_status, employer_name, 
        income_group, GroupID
    ) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)`;

    const values = [
        d.title_id, d.patient_name, d.age, d.gender, d.phone_no, d.email, d.dob || null, new Date(), 
        d.external_id, d.client_code, // FIXED: Correctly mapping these two
        d.door_no, d.flat_name, d.street_name1, d.street_name2, d.city, d.state, d.pincode, d.country,
        d.phone_home, d.locality, d.marital_status, d.notify_sms ? 1 : 0, d.notify_email ? 1 : 0,
        d.group_name, d.social_relationship, d.social_name, d.employment_status, d.employer_name, 
        d.income_group, 
        d.GroupID || null 
    ];

    db.query(sql, values, (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("Save Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.sqlMessage });
        }
        res.json({ success: true, message: "Record Saved!", id: result.insertId });
    });
});
