                                { l: 'Patient ID:', v: data.patient_id }, { l: 'Age / Sex:', v: data.age_sex },
                                { l: 'Sample ID:', v: data.sample_id }, { l: 'Client Code:', v: data.client_code },
                                { l: 'Referred By:', v: data.referred_by }, { l: 'External ID:', v: data.external_id },
                                { l: 'Collected At:', v: data.collected_at }
                            ].map((item, i) => (
                                <Grid item xs={12} sm={6} key={i} sx={{ display: 'flex', border: '0.5px solid #eee', p: 0.5 }}>
                                    <Typography sx={{ width: '130px', fontSize: '0.75rem', color: '#666' }}>{item.l}</Typography>
                                    <Typography sx={{ fontSize: '0.75rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>{item.v}</Typography>
                                </Grid>
                            ))}
                            <Grid item xs={12} sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', p: 0.8, borderTop: '1px solid #ccc', bgcolor: '#fafafa' }}>
                                <Typography sx={{ width: '130px', fontSize: '0.75rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Special Comments:</Typography>
                                <TextField size="small" fullWidth variant="outlined" sx={{ '& .MuiInputBase-input': { p: '4px 8px', fontSize: '0.75rem', bgcolor: 'white' } }} />
                                <Button variant="contained" size="small" sx={{ ml: 1, bgcolor: '#303f9f', fontSize: '0.65rem', textTransform: 'none' }}>Save Header</Button>
                            </Grid>
                        </Grid>
                    </Box>
                </Paper>

                {/* Status Bar */}
                <Box sx={{ maxWidth: 950, mx: 'auto', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end', alignItems: 'center', mb: 1, gap: 2 }}>
                    <Typography sx={{ color: '#4a148c', fontSize: '0.8rem', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>
                        Preview is available only after save of Samples!!
                    </Typography>
                    <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', bgcolor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)', px: 1, borderRadius: '4px' }}>
                        <Typography sx={{ fontSize: '0.7rem', color: 'white', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>Test Completed</Typography>
                        <RadioGroup row sx={{ ml: 1 }}>
                            <FormControlLabel value="yes" control={<Radio size="small" sx={{ color: 'white', '&.Mui-checked': { color: '#ffeb3b' } }} />} label={<Typography sx={{ fontSize: '0.7rem', color: 'white' }}>Yes</Typography>} />
                            <FormControlLabel value="no" control={<Radio size="small" sx={{ color: 'white', '&.Mui-checked': { color: '#ffeb3b' } }} />} label={<Typography sx={{ fontSize: '0.7rem', color: 'white' }}>No</Typography>} />
                        </RadioGroup>
                    </Box>
                    <Button variant="contained" startIcon={<AssessmentIcon />} sx={{ bgcolor: '#4a148c', textTransform: 'none', fontSize: '0.7rem', height: '30px' }}>View Report</Button>
                </Box>

                {/* Main Entry Table */}
<Paper sx={{ height: 420, width: '100%', maxWidth: 950, mx: 'auto', borderRadius: '4px', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
    <DataGrid
        rows={data.tests}
        columns={[
            { 
                field: 'name', 
                headerName: 'TName/EName', 
                flex: 1.5, 
                headerClassName: 'grid-header' 
            },
            { 
    field: 'value', 
    headerName: 'Input Value', 
    flex: 1, 
    renderCell: (params) => (
        <input 
            disabled={!editRows[params.id]} // Only enabled if in Edit mode
            defaultValue={params.value}
            id={`input-${params.id}`}
            style={{ 
                width: '90%', border: editRows[params.id] ? '2px solid #4a148c' : '1px solid #ccc', 
                textAlign: 'center', backgroundColor: editRows[params.id] ? '#fff' : '#f9f9f9' 
            }} 
        />
    )
},
            { 
                field: 'range', 
                headerName: 'Normal Range', 
                flex: 1, 
                align: 'center', 
                headerAlign: 'center' 
            },
            { 
                field: 'units', 
                headerName: 'Units', 
                flex: 0.8, 
                align: 'center', 
                headerAlign: 'center' 
            },
            { 
    field: 'comments', 
    headerName: 'Comments', 
    flex: 1.5, 
    renderCell: (params) => (
        <textarea 
            id={`comment-${params.id}`} 
            defaultValue={params.row.comments} // Pulls from your 'uniqueTestsMap'
            style={{ 
                width: '95%', 
                height: '35px', 
                border: '1px solid #ccc', 
                fontSize: '0.7rem',
                fontFamily: 'inherit'
            }} 
        />
    )
},
            { 
    field: 'history', 
    headerName: 'History', 
    flex: 1, 
    renderCell: (params) => (
        <Typography 
            onClick={() => {
                // Get the value currently typed in the input field
                const currentVal = document.getElementById(`input-${params.id}`)?.value;
                handleViewHistory(params.row.name, data.patient_id, currentVal);
            }}
            sx={{ 
                color: '#03a9f4', 
                cursor: 'pointer', 
                fontSize: '0.7rem', 
                textDecoration: 'underline'
            }}
        >
            View History
        </Typography>
    )
},
            { 
    field: 'actions', 
    headerName: 'Actions', 
    flex: 3, 
    renderCell: (params) => {
        const isEditing = editRows[params.id];
        const rowId = params.id;

        return (
            <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', gap: 0.5, alignItems: 'center' }}>
                {!isEditing ? (
                    <Button 
                        variant="outlined" size="small" color="primary" sx={{ fontSize: '0.6rem' }}
                        onClick={() => setEditRows(prev => ({ ...prev, [rowId]: true }))}
                    >Edit</Button>
                ) : (
                    <Button 
    variant="contained" size="small" color="success" 
    onClick={() => {
        const val = document.getElementById(`input-${rowId}`).value;
        const comm = document.getElementById(`comment-${rowId}`).value; // Fetch the comment
        handleAction(rowId, 'save', { value: val, comments: comm });
    }}
>Save</Button>
                )}

                <Button 
    variant="contained" size="small" sx={{ bgcolor: '#303f9f' }}
    onClick={() => {
        const val = document.getElementById(`input-${rowId}`).value;
        const comm = document.getElementById(`comment-${rowId}`).value; // Fetch the comment
        handleAction(rowId, 'confirm', { value: val, comments: comm });
    }}
>Confirm</Button>

                <Button 
                    variant="contained" size="small" color="error" sx={{ fontSize: '0.6rem' }}
                    onClick={() => handleAction(rowId, 'delete')}
                >Delete</Button>
                
                <Typography sx={{ 
                    color: params.row.status === 'Approved' ? 'green' : 'orange', 
                    fontSize: '0.65rem', fontWeight: 'bold', ml: 0.5 
                }}>
                    {params.row.status}
                </Typography>
            </Box>
        );
    }
}
        ]}
        initialState={{
            pagination: {
                paginationModel: { pageSize: 5 },
            },
        }}
        pageSizeOptions={[5]}
        rowHeight={50}
        disableRowSelectionOnClick
        sx={{
            '& .grid-header': { bgcolor: '#eeeeee', fontWeight: 'bold' },
            '& .MuiDataGrid-columnHeader': { bgcolor: '#eeeeee' },
            '& .MuiDataGrid-cell': { fontSize: '0.75rem', borderRight: '1px solid #eee' },
            // Custom Scrollbar styling
            '& ::-webkit-scrollbar': { width: '8px', height: '8px' },
            '& ::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb': { backgroundColor: '#bbb', borderRadius: '10px' },
            '& .MuiDataGrid-main': { overflow: 'auto' }
        }}
    />
</Paper>
            </Box>

            <Modal open={openHistory} onClose={() => setOpenHistory(false)}>
                <Box sx={{
                    position: 'absolute', top: '50%', left: '50%', transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)',
                    width: '90%', maxWidth: 650, bgcolor: 'white', boxShadow: 24, p: 3, borderRadius: 2
                }}>
                    <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', mb: 2 }}>
                        <Typography variant="h6" sx={{ color: '#4a148c', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>
                            Trend Analysis: {selectedTest}
                        </Typography>
                        <IconButton onClick={() => setOpenHistory(false)}><CloseIcon /></IconButton>
                    </Box>

                    <Box sx={{ width: '100%', height: 350, mt: 2 }}>
    {/* 1. Only render when Modal is open and Data exists */}
    {openHistory && historyData.length > 0 ? (
        <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="100%">
            <LineChart data={historyData} margin={{ top: 25, right: 30, left: 10, bottom: 10 }}>
    <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" vertical={false} stroke="#e0e0e0" />
    
    <XAxis 
        dataKey="date" 
        tick={{ fontSize: 12, fill: '#666' }} 
        axisLine={{ stroke: '#ccc' }}
        tickLine={false}
        dy={10}
    />
    
    <YAxis 
    tick={{ fontSize: 12, fill: '#666' }} 
    axisLine={{ stroke: '#ccc' }}
    tickLine={false}
    dx={-5}
    // Added padding (10%) so the line never touches the top or bottom edges
    domain={['dataMin - 1', 'dataMax + 1']} 
    allowDecimals={true}
/>
    
    <Tooltip 
        contentStyle={{ borderRadius: '8px', border: 'none', boxShadow: '0px 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)' }}
    />
    
   <Line 
    type="monotone"            // Smooth curves
    dataKey="value" 
    stroke="#4a148c"           // Patho Consult Purple
    strokeWidth={3} 
    dot={{ 
        r: 6, 
        fill: '#fff',          // White center (hollow look)
        stroke: '#4a148c',     // Purple border
        strokeWidth: 2 
    }} 
    activeDot={{ r: 8, fill: '#4a148c' }} 
    isAnimationActive={true}
    animationDuration={1200}
/>
</LineChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
    ) : (
        /* 2. Show this if no data is found */
        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', justifyContent: 'center', alignItems: 'center', height: '100%' }}>
            <Typography variant="body2" color="textSecondary">
                No previous history found for this test.
            </Typography>
        </Box>
    )}
</Box>
                    <Typography variant="caption" sx={{ display: 'block', mt: 2, textAlign: 'center', color: '#666' }}>
                        Showing last recorded values for Patient ID: {data.patient_id}
                    </Typography>
                </Box>
            </Modal>

            {/* Footer Address Bar */}
            <Box sx={{ position: 'fixed', bottom: 0, left: 0, right: 0, bgcolor: '#4a148c', color: 'white', py: 1, borderTop: '2px solid #4a148c' }}>
                <Typography sx={{ fontSize: '0.7rem', textAlign: 'center' }}>
                    63, Appu Street, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004. Phone: 044-24934435 | For Home Collection Contact: 044-24934435
                </Typography>
            </Box>
        </Box>
    );
}

// --- Main Component ---
function Home() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [selectedRole, setSelectedRole] = useState("");
  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false); 
  const [isAddModalOpen, setIsAddModalOpen] = useState(false); 

  // ADD THESE TWO LINES HERE:
  const [isRoleModalOpen, setIsRoleModalOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isSigModalOpen, setIsSigModalOpen] = useState(false);

  // ADD THIS FUNCTION BACK:
  const handleLogout = () => {
    localStorage.removeItem("userRole");
    localStorage.removeItem("userToken");
    navigate('/');
  };

  const handleActionClick = (itemName) => {
    if (itemName === "FrontDesk") {
      navigate('/frontdesk');
    } else if (itemName === "Sample Collect") {
      setIsModalOpen(true);
    } else if (itemName === "Customer Care") { 
      navigate('/customer-care'); // Correct place for Customer Care
    } else if (itemName === "PatientDetails") {
      navigate('/add-patient');
    } 
    else if (itemName === "Lab View") {
      navigate('/lab-view');
    }
     else if (itemName === "Approver ") {
      navigate('/approver');
    }
    else if (itemName === "TableView") {
      navigate('/table-view');
    }
    else if (itemName === "Ammend") {
      navigate('/ammend');
    }
    else {
      console.log(`${itemName} clicked`);
    }
  };

  const handleTableOpClick = (desc) => {
    if (desc === "Add Location Modal") {
      setIsAddModalOpen(true);
    } 
    else if (desc === "Add Role") {
      setIsRoleModalOpen(true);
    } 
    else if (desc === "Upload Signature") {
      setIsSigModalOpen(true);
    } 
    else if (desc === "Add Out Of Hospital") { 
      navigate('/add-out-of-hospital');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Group") {
      navigate('/add-group'); 
    }
    else if (desc === "View Location") {
      navigate('/view-location');
    } 
    else if (desc === "Create User") {
      navigate('/create-user');
    } 
    else if (desc === "Add Title") {
      navigate('/titles');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add CollectedAt") {
      navigate('/collected-at');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Insurance") {
      navigate('/add-insurance');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Doctors Details") {
      navigate('/add-doctor');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add PatientDetails") {
      navigate('/add-patient');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Client Code") {
      navigate('/add-client-code');
    }
    else if (desc === "Display Codes") {
      navigate('/display-codes'); 
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Test") {
      navigate('/add-test');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Profile") {
      navigate('/add-profile');
    }
    else if (desc === "Add Test Element") {
        navigate('/add-test-element');
    }
    else if (desc === "Edit Rate Card") {
        navigate('/edit-rate-card');
    }
     else if (desc === "Lab View") {
        navigate('/lab-view');
     }
     else if (desc === "Template Details") {
        navigate('/template-details');
     }
     else if (desc === "Disable Test") {
        navigate('/disable-test');
     }
     else if (desc === "View Edit Test") {
        navigate('/view-edit-test');
     }
     else if (desc === "Add Department") {
        navigate('/add-department');
     }
     else if (desc === "Department Priority") {
        navigate('/department-priority');
     }
     else if (desc === "Add Department Priority") {
        navigate('/add-department-priority');
     }
     else if (desc === "Add Test Priority") {
        navigate('/add-test-priority');
     }
     else if (desc === "Add Free Text Template") {
        navigate('/add-free-text-template');
     }
     else if (desc === "Add Isolated Organism") {
        navigate('/add-isolated-organs');
     }
     else if (desc === "Add AntiMicrobial Agent") {
        navigate('/add-microbial-agent');
     }
     else if (desc === "Edit Invoice") {
        navigate('/edit-invoice');
     }
     else if (desc === "Invoice Report") {
    navigate('/invoice-report'); 
  }
  else if (desc === "Camp Report") {
        navigate('/camp-report');
     }
    else {
      alert(`${desc} module is coming soon!`);
    }
  };

  const handleModalSubmit = (code) => {
    setIsModalOpen(false);
    navigate('/sample-collect', { state: { locationCode: code } });
  };

  return (
    <div className="home-wrapper">
      <header className="brand-nav" style={{ 
    backgroundColor: '#4a148c', 
    display: 'flex', 
    alignItems: 'center', 
    padding: '10px 20px',
    color: 'white',
    position: 'relative' 
}}>
  {/* 1. Left Spacer (matches the width of the right section to keep title dead-center) */}
  <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
     {/* You can put a logo or home icon here if needed later */}
  </div>

  {/* 2. Center Title */}
  <h3 className="nav-title" style={{ 
      margin: 0, 
      textAlign: 'center',

      whiteSpace: 'nowrap' 
  }}>
      Patho Consult
  </h3>
  
  {/* 3. Right Section */}
  <div className="nav-right-section" style={{ flex: 1, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
    <button 
      className="logout-btn-box"

      style={{

      }}

      onMouseOut={(e) => e.target.style.backgroundColor = '#ffffff'}
    >
      Logout
    </button>
  </div>
</header>
      <main className="dashboard-content">
        <h2 className="welcome-banner">Welcome To Patho Clinic</h2>
        
        <section className="admin-panel">
          <div className="panel-row">

            <select 
              className="purple-select"

              onChange={(e) => setSelectedRole(e.target.value)}
            >
              <option value="">-- Select User Role --</option>
              <option value="Admin">Admin</option>
              <option value="Registration">Registration</option>
              <option value="Lab">Lab</option>
              <option value="Invoice">Invoice</option>
            </select>
          </div>

          {selectedRole && (
  <Box sx={{ mt: 3, width: '100%' }}>
    <TableContainer 
  component={Paper} 
  sx={{ 
    maxHeight: 440, 
    boxShadow: '0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)',
    borderRadius: '8px',
    overflow: 'auto',
    
    // 1. The Main Scrollbar Area
    '&::-webkit-scrollbar': { 
      width: '12px', // Slightly wider to accommodate arrows comfortably
    },
    
    // 2. The Track (the background)
    '&::-webkit-scrollbar-track': { 
      backgroundColor: '#f3e5f5', 
      borderRadius: '10px'
    },
    
    // 3. The Draggable Handle (The Line)
    '&::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb': {

      border: '2px solid #f3e5f5', // Creates padding around the "line"

    },

    // 4. The Up and Down Arrows (Buttons)
    '&::-webkit-scrollbar-button:single-button': {
      backgroundColor: '#f3e5f5',
      display: 'block',
      backgroundSize: '10px',
      backgroundRepeat: 'no-repeat',
    },
    
    // Up Arrow Icon
    '&::-webkit-scrollbar-button:single-button:vertical:decrement': {
      height: '12px',
      width: '12px',
      backgroundPosition: 'center 4px',
      backgroundImage: `url("data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg' width='100' height='100' fill='%234a148c'><polygon points='50,0 0,100 100,100'/></svg>")`,
    },

    // Down Arrow Icon
    '&::-webkit-scrollbar-button:single-button:vertical:increment': {
      height: '12px',
      width: '12px',
      backgroundPosition: 'center 2px',
      backgroundImage: `url("data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg' width='100' height='100' fill='%234a148c'><polygon points='0,0 100,0 50,100'/></svg>")`,
    }
  }}
>
      <Table stickyHeader aria-label="sticky table" size="small">
        <TableHead>
          <TableRow>
            <TableCell sx={{ bgcolor: '#4a148c !important', color: 'white', fontWeight: 'bold', width: '80px' }}>
              S.No
            </TableCell>
            <TableCell sx={{ bgcolor: '#4a148c !important', color: 'white', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>

            </TableCell>

              Action
            </TableCell>
          </TableRow>
        </TableHead>
        <TableBody>
          {roleOperations[selectedRole].map((op) => (

              hover 
              sx={{ '&:nth-of-type(even)': { bgcolor: '#f3e5f5' } }}
            >
              <TableCell sx={{ fontSize: '13px' }}>{op.sNo}</TableCell>
              <TableCell sx={{ fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 500 }}>{op.desc}</TableCell>
              <TableCell sx={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>
                <button 
                  className="view-page-btn"
                  onClick={() => handleTableOpClick(op.desc)}
                  style={{
                    padding: '4px 12px',
                    fontSize: '12px',
                    cursor: 'pointer'
                  }}
                >
                  {op.page}
                </button>
              </TableCell>
            </TableRow>
          ))}
        </TableBody>
      </Table>
    </TableContainer>
    
    <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', mt: 2 }}>
    <button className="innovative-btn">Trigger Cron</button>
</Box>
  </Box>
)}
        </section>

        <div className="action-list">
          {menuItems.map((item) => (
            <div 
              key={item.name} 
              className="action-row" 
              onClick={() => handleActionClick(item.name)}
            >
              <span className="action-text">
                {item.name} 
                {item.badge && <span className="purple-badge">{item.badge}</span>}
              </span>
              <span className="action-chevron">›</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </main>

      {/* --- MODALS SECTION --- */}
      {/* 1. Find Location */}
      <LocationModal 
        isOpen={isModalOpen} 
        onClose={() => setIsModalOpen(false)} 
        onConfirm={handleModalSubmit}
      />

      {/* 2. Add Location */}
      <AddLocationModal 
        isOpen={isAddModalOpen} 
        onClose={() => setIsAddModalOpen(false)} 
      />

      {/* 3. Add Role */}
      <AddRoleModal 
        isOpen={isRoleModalOpen} 
        onClose={() => setIsRoleModalOpen(false)} 
      />

      {/* 4. Upload Signature */}
      <UploadSignatureModal 
        isOpen={isSigModalOpen} 
        onClose={() => setIsSigModalOpen(false)} 
      />
      
      <footer className="footer-bar">
        System Status: Secure | Connected to Diagnostics Cloud
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

export default Home;

function Home() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [selectedRole, setSelectedRole] = useState("Admin");
  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false); 
  const [isAddModalOpen, setIsAddModalOpen] = useState(false); 
  const [isRoleModalOpen, setIsRoleModalOpen] = useState(false);
  const [isSigModalOpen, setIsSigModalOpen] = useState(false);

  const handleLogout = () => {
    localStorage.removeItem("userRole");
    localStorage.removeItem("userToken");
    navigate('/');
  };
  const [userProfile, setUserProfile] = useState({
    name: "User",
    role: "Staff"
  });

  // 2. Fetch data from storage on load
  useEffect(() => {
    const storedName = localStorage.getItem("userName");
    const storedRole = localStorage.getItem("userRole");

    if (storedName && storedRole) {
      setUserProfile({
        name: storedName,
        role: storedRole
      });
      
      // Optional: Auto-select the table view based on their role
      if (roleOperations[storedRole]) {
        setSelectedRole(storedRole);
      }
    }
  }, []);

  const handleActionClick = (itemName) => {
    if (itemName === "FrontDesk") navigate('/frontdesk');
    else if (itemName === "Sample Collect") setIsModalOpen(true);
    else if (itemName === "Customer Care") navigate('/customer-care');
    else if (itemName === "PatientDetails") navigate('/add-patient');
    else if (itemName === "Lab View") navigate('/lab-view');
    else if (itemName === "Approver ") navigate('/approver');
    else if (itemName === "TableView") navigate('/table-view');
    else if (itemName === "Ammend") navigate('/ammend');
    else console.log(`${itemName} clicked`);
  };

  const handleTableOpClick = (desc) => {
    // Navigation Map for Table Actions
    const navigationMap = {
      "Add Location Modal": () => setIsAddModalOpen(true),
      "Add Role": () => setIsRoleModalOpen(true),
      "Upload Signature": () => setIsSigModalOpen(true),
      "Add Out Of Hospital": '/add-out-of-hospital',
      "Add Group": '/add-group',
      "View Location": '/view-location',
      "Create User": '/create-user',
      "Add Title": '/titles',
      "Add CollectedAt": '/collected-at',
      "Add Insurance": '/add-insurance',
      "Add Doctors Details": '/add-doctor',
      "Add PatientDetails": '/add-patient',
      "Add Client Code": '/add-client-code',
      "Display Codes": '/display-codes',
      "Add Test": '/add-test',
      "Add Profile": '/add-profile',
      "Add Test Element": '/add-test-element',
      "Edit Rate Card": '/edit-rate-card',
      "Lab View": '/lab-view',
      "Template Details": '/template-details',
      "Disable Test": '/disable-test',
      "View Edit Test": '/view-edit-test',
      "Add Department": '/add-department',
      "Department Priority": '/department-priority',
      "Add Department Priority": '/add-department-priority',
      "Add Test Priority": '/add-test-priority',
      "Add Free Text Template": '/add-free-text-template',
      "Add Isolated Organism": '/add-isolated-organs',
      "Add AntiMicrobial Agent": '/add-microbial-agent',
      "Edit Invoice": '/edit-invoice',
      "Invoice Report": '/invoice-report',
      "Camp Report": '/camp-report'
    };

    const target = navigationMap[desc];
    if (typeof target === 'function') target();
    else if (typeof target === 'string') navigate(target);
    else alert(`${desc} module is coming soon!`);
  };

  return (
    <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', bgcolor: '#f3e5f5', minHeight: '100vh' }}>

            color: 'white',
            borderRight: 'none'
          },
        }}

        <Box sx={{ p: 3, textAlign: 'center', background: 'linear-gradient(45deg, #4a148c 30%, #7b1fa2 90%)' }}>
          <Typography variant="h6" fontWeight="800">PATHO PRO</Typography>
          <Typography variant="caption" sx={{ opacity: 0.7 }}>DIAGNOSTICS v2.0</Typography>
        </Box>
        
        <List sx={{ mt: 2, px: 1 }}>
          {menuItems.map((item) => (
            <ListItemButton 
              key={item.name}
              onClick={() => handleActionClick(item.name)}
              sx={{ borderRadius: '8px', mb: 0.5, '&:hover': { bgcolor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)' } }}
            >
              <ListItemIcon sx={{ color: '#ce93d8', minWidth: 40 }}>{item.icon}</ListItemIcon>
              <ListItemText primary={item.name} primaryTypographyProps={{ fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 500 }} />
              {item.badge && <Badge badgeContent={item.badge} color="secondary" sx={{ ml: 1 }} />}

          ))}

        <Box sx={{ mt: 'auto', p: 2 }}>
          <ListItemButton onClick={handleLogout} sx={{ borderRadius: '8px', color: '#ff8a80' }}>
            <ListItemIcon sx={{ color: '#ff8a80', minWidth: 40 }}><Logout /></ListItemIcon>

        </Box>

      <Box component="main" sx={{ flexGrow: 1, p: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}>

<Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', p: 2, px: 4, bgcolor: 'white', borderBottom: '1px solid #e0e0e0' }}>
  <Typography variant="h5" fontWeight="700" color="#4a148c">Patho Consult</Typography>

app.delete('/api/delete-test', (req, res) => {
    const { sampleId, testName } = req.body;

    if (!sampleId || !testName) {
        return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: "Missing sampleId or testName" });
    }

    const cleanTestName = testName.trim();

    // 1. Get the current string of tests
    const getSql = "SELECT id, test_names FROM patient_billing_details WHERE sample_id = ?";
    
    db.query(getSql, [sampleId], (err, results) => {
        if (err || results.length === 0) {
            return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: "Record not found" });
        }

        const record = results[0];
        const currentTests = record.test_names;

        // 2. Remove the specific test from the comma-separated string
        // This splits the string, filters out the one you want to delete, and joins it back
        const updatedTests = currentTests
            .split(',')
            .map(t => t.trim())
            .filter(t => t !== cleanTestName)
            .join(', ');

        // 3. If no tests are left, delete the row. Otherwise, update the string.
        if (updatedTests === "") {
            const deleteSql = "DELETE FROM patient_billing_details WHERE id = ?";
            db.query(deleteSql, [record.id], (delErr) => {
                if (delErr) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: delErr.message });
                res.json({ success: true, message: "Row deleted (last test removed)" });
            });
        } else {
            const updateSql = "UPDATE patient_billing_details SET test_names = ? WHERE id = ?";
            db.query(updateSql, [updatedTests, record.id], (upErr) => {
                if (upErr) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: upErr.message });
                res.json({ success: true, message: "Test removed, others preserved" });
            });
        }
    });
});












app.get('/api/patient-history/:patientId', (req, res) => {
    const { patientId } = req.params;

    const sql = `
        SELECT 
            p.patient_name,
            p.PatientID,
            DATE_FORMAT(pb.bill_date, '%Y-%m-%d') AS date,
            /* Get the long string of tests from the groups table if it exists */
            g.ProfileTest AS profileTests,
            /* Fallback name from billing or master test table */
            COALESCE(tm.TestName, pb.group_name) AS fallbackName,
            pb.culture_report AS value, 
            pb.Status AS billingStatus,
            tm.Units AS directUnits
        FROM patient_billing_details pb
        JOIN patients p ON pb.PatientID = p.PatientID
        LEFT JOIN tests tm ON pb.TestID = tm.TestID
        LEFT JOIN \`groups\` g ON pb.group_name = g.GroupName
        WHERE p.PatientID = ?
        ORDER BY pb.bill_date ASC;
    `;

    db.query(sql, [patientId], async (err, results) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
        if (results.length === 0) return res.json({ success: true, data: { records: [] } });

        // Fetch all test units once to use for lookup when splitting profiles
        const [allTests] = await db.promise().query("SELECT TestName, Units FROM tests");
        const unitMap = {};
        allTests.forEach(t => { unitMap[t.TestName] = t.Units; });

        const processedRecords = [];

       results.forEach(row => {
    // 1. Extract the first sequence of numbers/decimals (e.g., "12.5" from "12.5 mg/dL")
    const match = row.value ? String(row.value).match(/(\d+(\.\d+)?)/) : null;
    const parsedValue = match ? parseFloat(match[0]) : null;
    
    // 2. Strict check: only assign if it's a real number
    const numericValue = (parsedValue !== null && !isNaN(parsedValue)) ? parsedValue : null;

    const baseData = {
        date: row.date,
        value: row.value || 'N/A',
        numericValue: numericValue, 
        status: row.billingStatus
    };

            // If it's a group/camp with multiple tests in ProfileTest
            if (row.profileTests) {
                // Remove prefix like "PR5007-" or "TEST-" if present, then split by comma
                const cleanTests = row.profileTests.replace(/(PR\d+-|TEST-)/g, '');
                cleanTests.split(',').forEach(name => {
                    const trimmedName = name.trim();
                    processedRecords.push({
                        ...baseData,
                        testName: trimmedName,
                        units: unitMap[trimmedName] || row.directUnits || 'N/A'
                    });
                });
            } else {
                // Single test logic
                processedRecords.push({
                    ...baseData,
                    testName: row.fallbackName || 'General Test',
                    units: row.directUnits || 'N/A'
                });
            }
        });

        res.json({
            success: true,
            data: {
                patientName: results[0].patient_name,
                patientId: results[0].PatientID,
                records: processedRecords
            }
        });
    });
});









app.post('/api/save-billing', (req, res) => {
    const { invoice_no, sample_id, billingRecords } = req.body;

    if (!billingRecords || billingRecords.length === 0) {
        return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: "No records provided" });
    }

    // Map the values for the bulk insert
    const values = billingRecords.map(record => [
        record.PatientID, 
        record.TestID || 0, 
        record.Status || 'Pending', 
        parseFloat(record.Amount || 0), 
        record.billing_type || 'group',
        record.location_code || 'G-01', 
        record.doctor_id || null, 
        parseFloat(record.amount_paid || 0), 
        record.payment_modes || 'Cash', 
        invoice_no,
        sample_id, 
        record.patient_name, 
        parseFloat(record.balance || 0), 
        record.collected_at_id || null, 
        record.client_code, 
        record.group_name,
        record.insurance_payer || null,
        record.policy_no || record.policy_number || null, 
        record.hospital_id || record.hospital_name || null, 
        new Date() // payment_date
    ]);

    const sql = `
        INSERT INTO patient_billing_details 
        (PatientID, TestID, Status, Amount, billing_type, location_code, doctor_id, 
         amount_paid, payment_modes, invoice_no, sample_id, patient_name, balance, 
         collected_at_id, client_code, group_name, insurance_payer, policy_number, 
         hospital_name, payment_date) 
        VALUES ?
        ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE 
            Status = VALUES(Status),
            Amount = VALUES(Amount),
            amount_paid = VALUES(amount_paid),
            balance = VALUES(balance),
            payment_modes = VALUES(payment_modes),
            sample_id = VALUES(sample_id),
            payment_date = VALUES(payment_date)`;

    db.query(sql, [values], (err, result) => {
        if (err) {
            console.error("SQL Error:", err);
            return res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });
        }
        res.json({ 
            success: true, 
            message: "Invoice Processed Successfully", 
            affectedRows: result.affectedRows 
        });
    });
});
app.get('/api/registration-metadata', (req, res) => {
    const titlesQuery = "SELECT id, title_name FROM titles";
    const doctorsQuery = "SELECT id, doctor_name FROM doctor_details"; 

    db.query(titlesQuery, (err, titleResults) => {
        if (err) return res.status(500).json(err);
        db.query(doctorsQuery, (err, doctorResults) => {
            if (err) return res.status(500).json(err);
            res.json({ 
                titles: titleResults, 
                doctors: doctorResults 
            });
        });
    });
});

+-----+-----------+--------+------------+----------+---------+--------------+---------------+-----------+-------------+-----------------+------------------+---------------+---------------------+-------------------+-----------+--------------+---------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+---------------------+--------------+-----------------+-------------+---------------------------+-----------------------+---------------+---------------+----------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------+-------------+-------------+-------------+app.get('/api/sample-details/:sampleId', (req, res) => {

    const { sampleId } = req.params;



    const sql = `

        SELECT 

            p.patient_name, 

            b.LabComments,

            p.PatientID AS patient_id, 

            p.age AS Age, 

            p.gender AS Gender, 

            p.external_id, 

            -- FIXED: This looks at billing first, then patient table as fallback

            COALESCE(b.client_code, p.client_code) AS client_code, 

            DATE_FORMAT(p.RegDate, '%d-%m-%Y %H:%i') AS registration_date,

            b.id AS billing_id, 

            b.sample_id, 

            b.Status AS test_status, 

            b.Amount AS price,

            b.ResultValue,

            COALESCE(t.TestName, b.group_name, 'Unknown Test') AS test_display_name,

            COALESCE(d.doctor_name, 'Self') AS referredBy,

            tem.unit AS element_unit,

            CONCAT(COALESCE(tem.lower_limit, ''), '-', COALESCE(tem.upper_limit, '')) AS element_range,

            tt.test_content

        FROM patient_billing_details b

        INNER JOIN patients p ON b.PatientID = p.PatientID

        LEFT JOIN tests t ON b.TestID = t.TestID

        LEFT JOIN doctor_details d ON b.doctor_id = d.id

        LEFT JOIN test_element_templates tem ON b.TestID = tem.element_id 

        LEFT JOIN test_templates tt ON b.TestID = tt.test_id

        WHERE b.sample_id = ?

    `;



    db.query(sql, [sampleId], (err, results) => {

        if (err) return res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Database error" });

        if (results.length === 0) return res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: "No records found" });



        const tests = results.map(row => {

            let normalRange = (row.element_range && row.element_range !== '-') ? row.element_range : "-";

            let units = row.element_unit || "N/A";

            



            if ((normalRange === "-" || units === "N/A") && row.test_content) {

                try {

                    const content = JSON.parse(row.test_content);

                    if (Array.isArray(content) && content.length > 0) {

                        normalRange = content[0].range || normalRange;

                        units = content[0].unit || units;

                    }

                } catch (e) { console.error("JSON error", e); }

            }



            return {

                billing_id: row.billing_id,

                test_name: row.test_display_name,

                status: row.test_status,

                ResultValue: row.ResultValue || "-", 

                LabComments: row.LabComments || "",

                normal_range: normalRange,

                Units: units.trim()

            };

        });



        const patientData = {

            patient_name: results[0].patient_name,

            patient_id: results[0].patient_id,

            age: results[0].Age,

            gender: results[0].Gender,

            external_id: results[0].external_id,

            client_code: results[0].client_code || "N/A", 

            registration_date: results[0].registration_date,

            sample_id: results[0].sample_id,

            referredBy: results[0].referredBy,

            tests: tests

        };



        res.json({ success: true, data: patientData });

    });

});here patient with test only fecth test name and range and other details but for profile it is not fetching
